# Strict-Typing Agent Team Registry

Live state of parallel agents working on the strict-typing plan
(`~/.claude/plans/stop-native-vs-tagged-tax.md`). One row per worker. Update
this file at every state transition (start of cluster, close of cluster,
blocked). The supervisor reviews this before dispatching new work.

## Why this exists

Two-or-more agents working in parallel on `bulldozer-strictly-typed` can
collide on shared territory (`type_schema/mod.rs`, `json_value.rs`,
marshal-layer files). Cluster-close merges already collided once on
`docs/defections.md`. This registry is the cheapest possible coordination
surface: agents declare intent up front; the supervisor catches overlap
before it's coded.

Each variant funnels through it with the appropriate `(wrap_targets, self_arg_positions)` descriptors — `Direct`/`Generic` empty; `BoxedReturn` populates `wrap_targets`; `SelfArg` populates `self_arg_positions`; `Compound` populates both. Dispatch sequence: (1) **SelfArg identity check** per §Q25.C.2 — for each `pos ∈ self_arg_positions`, peek the arg slot at `receiver_idx + 1 + pos`, verify it's a `Ptr(HeapKind::TraitObject)` and that its `vtable` Arc matches the receiver's via `TraitObjectStorage::vtable_eq` (`Arc::ptr_eq` on the vtable Arcs is the canonical equality). Non-TraitObject arg kind or mismatched vtable surfaces a structured `VMError::RuntimeError` citing §Q25.C.2. (2) **Argument lowering** — replace receiver and each Self-arg slot's `dyn` carrier with the inner `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` via `stack_write_kinded` (drops the previous TraitObject share, installs the new TypedObject share). (3) **Call** — route through `call_function_with_nb_args` + `execute_until_call_depth` per the canonical call path. (4) **Return wrap** per §Q25.C.1 — `rewrap_return_value(ret_bits, ret_kind, wrap_targets, receiver_vtable)` walks every `WrapTarget::path` through the return value and re-boxes at each leaf. **Generic dispatch**: Shape's bytecode tier treats generic methods as type-erased at the impl's function-id (no per-call-site monomorphization), so `Generic` collapses to Direct dispatch at the bytecode layer — the `TypeInfo` parameter in the §Q25.C.3 spec is metadata for the thunk to dispatch operations on `g`, not a separate bytecode argument. The deferred per-call-site monomorphization amendment shape is documented in-code at the `Generic` arm. **Nested BoxedReturn** (`rewrap_return_value`): dispatches on the structural carrier's `NativeKind`. `Result<T, Self>`-shaped returns descend via `rewrap_result_payload` — selects the wrap-target arm matching `is_ok`, rewraps the `KindedSlot payload` if path matches. `Option<Self>` via `rewrap_option_payload` — single-arm, rewraps Some.payload if path=[0]. `Array<Self>` via `rewrap_typed_array_elements` — rebuilds the buffer as `TypedArrayData::TraitObject(Arc<TypedBuffer<Arc<TraitObjectStorage>>>)` with each element rewrapped using the receiver's vtable. `TypedObject` (tuples/records per C+ rewire) and `HashMap<K, Self>` — surface-and-stop with structured error citing §Q25.C.5: in-place tuple/record-field and HashMap-values-buffer rewrap pending typed-buffer write-path integration (see `TypedObjectStorage::write_slot_in_place` from W17-references-mutation per hardening §c, and `HashMapValueBuf::TraitObject` arm). The dispatch shell stays correct — these surfaces only fire when the emission tier emits wrap-targets for those carrier shapes, which the round-3 compiler-classification path doesn't currently do (it surfaces structural errors for tuples/maps already if the trait return shape includes them). **`Closure` variant**: surface-and-stop with structured error citing §Q25.C.5 + §2.7.11/Q12. The W7 closure-trait-impl emission tier doesn't currently construct `VTableEntry::Closure` entries, so the dispatch arm is reachable only via a future W17-trait-object-closure-call sub-cluster; surfacing keeps the variant's contract visible without faking a closure-call. **Compiler-side wrap-target classification** (`build_and_register_vtable`): replaced the round-2 binary "top-level Self vs `has_nested_self` → Compound surface" with a `collect_self_wrap_targets` walker that traces the generic-arg-index path through `TypeAnnotation::Generic` / `Tuple` / `Array` and pushes a proper `WrapTarget` for every Self site (path=[] for top-level, path=[0] for Option/Array element / Result Ok arm, path=[1] for HashMap value / Result Err arm, deeper paths for nesting). The `ThunkSignature::build` call then dispatches the appropriate `VTableEntry::*` variant via `to_vtable_entry` — Direct when no flags, single-shape when one flag, `Compound` when multiple. 7 wrap-target-walker unit tests pin the §Q25.C.1 row contracts (top-level Self / concrete / Result-of-Self / Option-of-Self / HashMap<K, Self> / Tuple<Self, Self> / nested Option<Result<Self, E>> / Array<Self>). **13 thunks smoke tests** in `executor/tests/trait_object_thunks.rs`: Direct (sanity), BoxedReturn(top-level), SelfArg-same-impl (accepts), SelfArg-cross-impl (handles cleanly, panic-free), Option<Self>, Result<Self, E>, Generic, Closure-by-absence (Plain trait without closure variants runs cleanly), nested-path walk (Result<Self, Self>), Array<Self> elements, receiver share-lifecycle (multiple uses), kind dispatch after boxing. | `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w17-trait-object-emission` | `../shape-w17-trait-object-emission` | W17-trait-object-emission — compiler-side dyn-coerce grammar + emit + DynMethodCall (the BoxTraitObject upstream gap) | — | Pest grammar for `dyn`-coerce syntax (verify or extend), type inference for dyn coercion, bytecode emit for `OpCode::BoxTraitObject` + `OpCode::DynMethodCall`, compiler-side vtable lookup at coerce-to-dyn time. End-to-end §2.7.24 Q25.C smoke: `let a: dyn Animal = box(Dog{...}); print(a.name())`. | **closed** (Wave-2.6 round-2 close 2026-05-11; emission-tier compiler+runtime half of ADR-006 §2.7.24 Q25.C landed end-to-end per the rescope contract — the 4 SURFACE bodies in `executor/trait_object_ops.rs` (BoxTraitObject / DynMethodCall / DropCall / DropCallAsync) replaced with real implementations, dyn-coerce sites in `let a: dyn T = ...` emit `OpCode::BoxTraitObject` with trait-name `Operand::Name`, dyn-method-call sites in `a.method()` (where `a` is dyn-tracked) emit `OpCode::DynMethodCall` with `TypedMethodCall` operand. Grammar: `TypeAnnotation::Dyn(traits)` already parses via `dyn_type = "dyn" ~ qualified_ident ~ ("+" ~ qualified_ident)*` in `crates/shape-ast/src/shape.pest:864`; no grammar extension needed. Type inference: dyn-typed locals tracked in two new `HashMap<u16, String>` maps on `BytecodeCompiler` (`dyn_locals` / `dyn_module_bindings`) keyed by slot index → trait name, populated at `Statement::VariableDecl` for both function-local and module-binding paths. Bytecode emit: `compile_expr_method_call` (`expressions/function_calls.rs`) checks `Expr::Identifier` receivers against these maps BEFORE compiling the receiver (since `compile_expr` overwrites `last_expr_*` state); when the receiver is dyn-tracked, emits `DynMethodCall` instead of `CallMethod`. Compile-tier vtable construction: new `compiler/trait_object_emission.rs` exposes `build_and_register_vtable` called from `register_item_functions` at `Item::Impl` entry; walks impl methods, classifies each via `Erase_T` (top-level `Self` in return → `BoxedReturn` w/ `wrap_targets=[path=[]]`; no Self / no generics → `Direct`; nested Self or Self-arg or method-generics → `Compound` with flags set, surface-and-stop at dispatch). Vtables stored in new `program.trait_vtables: HashMap<String, Arc<VTable>>` keyed by `"Trait::ConcreteType"`. Threaded through Program→ContentAddressedProgram→LinkedProgram→BytecodeProgram via per-step `.clone()` + propagated through `load_linked_program` and `linked_to_bytecode_program`. Bytecode-cache integration: `BytecodeCache::put` skips caching for trait-bearing programs (same pattern as the closure-bearing skip — `Arc<VTable>` is `#[serde(skip)]`). Runtime: `op_box_trait_object` recovers `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` via canonical `Arc::from_raw` (3ac2f11 pattern), looks up `Arc<VTable>` from program registry, allocates `Arc<TraitObjectStorage>` and pushes via `push_kinded(bits, Ptr(HeapKind::TraitObject))`. `op_dyn_method_call` recovers `Arc<TraitObjectStorage>` via transient borrow, resolves the impl function name via runtime `trait_method_symbols` lookup (`Trait::Type::__default__::method` → function name) + `function_name_index` → runtime function id (post-link), then dispatches per `VTableEntry` variant. `op_call_method` was extended with a TraitObject receiver fast-path that re-routes to the dyn dispatch shell — handles the `let b = a.clone_me()` case where the compiler doesn't yet propagate `dyn T` through method-call result types (compile-tier follow-up; deferred). `op_drop_call_sync` / `op_drop_call_async` look up `Drop::<TypeName>::__default__::drop` / `drop_async` from `trait_method_symbols`; silent no-op if no Drop impl is registered (the kinded pop already retired the share). End-to-end smoke on `--mode vm` (after `rm -rf ~/.shape/cache/bytecode` to invalidate stale cache): `let a: dyn Animal = Dog { name: "Rex" }; print(a.name()); let b = a.clone_me(); print(b.name())` → prints `Rex\nRex`. Direct dispatch (`name()`) and BoxedReturn dispatch (`clone_me()`) both verified. **Deferred** (in-scope but surfaced-and-stopped): `VTableEntry::SelfArg` (§Q25.C.2 Self-in-arg runtime vtable-identity check), `Generic` (§Q25.C.3 method-generic TypeInfo threading), `Compound` (§Q25.C.5 multi-flag thunk), `BoxedReturn` with nested wrap-targets (`Result<Self,E>`, `Option<Self>`, `(Self,Self)`, etc.) — each surfaces as `VMError::NotImplemented(SURFACE: ... per ADR-006 §Q25.C.5 ...)` at `op_dyn_method_call` dispatch time. `Closure` variant (W7 closure-trait-impl dispatch) deferred. IC devirtualization per §Q25.C.6 deferred (round-2 budget). LSP cost-class inlay hints per §Q25.C.7 deferred. | `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w17-comptime-vm-dispatch` | `../shape-w17-comptime-vm-dispatch` | W17-comptime-vm-dispatch — rebuild `populate_module_objects` so the compiled bytecode chain `LoadModuleBinding + GetFieldTyped + CallValue` dispatches through TypedObject module-bindings storing function-id field references | — | `executor/vm_impl/modules.rs::populate_module_objects` (no-op stub → kinded TypedObject construction) + `executor/typed_object_ops.rs::op_get_field_typed` (canonical 5-arm receiver-recovery soundness fix + FIELD_TAG_ANY → field_kinds resolver) + `executor/call_convention.rs::call_value_immediate_nb` (new `NativeKind::Ptr(HeapKind::ModuleFn)` dispatch arm) + new `HeapKind::ModuleFn=33` pure-discriminator HeapKind with 4-table lockstep | **closed** (Wave-3 close 2026-05-12; ADR-006 §2.7.26 amendment landed — module-function-id inline-scalar HeapKind ordinal 33 added to fill the upstream dispatch blocker flagged by W17-snapshot-roundtrip (`fbfbfb6`). **`populate_module_objects` rebuild shape**: iterates `module_registry.modules()` (33 native modules at populate time), for each: collects sync `TypedModuleFunction` + async `TypedModuleAsyncFunction` exports, registers each into `module_fn_table` via `register_module_fn_entry` to obtain a `module_fn_id`, looks up the predeclared `__mod_<name>` schema (registered by the compiler's `ensure_module_object_schema`), builds slots in schema field order — each callable field gets `ValueSlot::from_raw(fn_id as u64)` with `field_kinds[i] = NativeKind::Ptr(HeapKind::ModuleFn)` and heap_mask bit set; unmatched fields get the `(0, NativeKind::Bool)` sentinel pair. Constructs `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` via the typed `TypedObjectStorage::new` per ADR-006 §2.4 + writes through `module_binding_write_kinded(binding_idx, bits, Ptr(TypedObject))` per §2.7.8/Q10 lockstep. Binding-name resolution: prefers the hidden `__imported_module__::<name>` binding (compiler-injected by `ensure_hidden_native_module_binding`) and falls back to the plain name. Modules with no `__mod_<name>` schema are silently skipped — the binding stays at the no-op sentinel and any reference will surface clean at GetFieldTyped. **Dispatch chain end-to-end**: (1) `LoadModuleBinding(idx)` reads the populated TypedObject via `module_binding_read_kinded_raw` and pushes via `clone_with_kind` retain-on-read (§2.7.7); (2) `GetFieldTyped { type_id, field_idx, field_type_tag=FIELD_TAG_ANY }` recovers `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` via canonical `Arc::<X>::from_raw` (3ac2f11 precedent — the pre-W17 `as_heap_value()` cast was wrong-type recovery on `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` bits and segfaulted on schema_id alignment with HeapKind discriminator ordinals), then routes the FIELD_TAG_ANY operand to new helper `push_field_value_with_kind(slot, kind)` which sources the kind from `storage.field_kinds[i]` rather than the schema (resolves hardening item (f) — "`Any → Dynamic` readback bounded by `KindedSlot.kind`"); pushes `(module_fn_id as u64, NativeKind::Ptr(HeapKind::ModuleFn))`; (3) `CallValue` pops args + callee, dispatches via `call_value_immediate_nb`'s new `Ptr(HeapKind::ModuleFn)` arm which routes `bits as usize` to `invoke_module_fn_id_stub(fn_id, args)` (the upstream stub W17-snapshot-roundtrip wired at `fbfbfb6`). **Smoke results (6 W17 unit tests, all pass)**: `w17_comptime_arithmetic_sanity` (regression — comptime arithmetic still works after populate_module_objects rebuild); `w17_comptime_build_config_dispatches_end_to_end` (dispatch reaches body cleanly — body itself crashes on a pre-existing `kinded.slot().as_heap_value()` wrong-type recovery on `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` bits in `comptime_builtins.rs:282`, fixed in this commit using canonical `Arc::<TypedObjectStorage>::from_raw` pattern — same 5-arm soundness rule); `w17_comptime_implements_dispatches_end_to_end` (returns Bool false for unregistered trait); `w17_comptime_warning_dispatches_end_to_end` (returns Unit, body emits stderr); `w17_comptime_error_dispatches_end_to_end` (returns Err with `[comptime error]` prefix — arg-kind marshalling shim arg-as-Bool is pre-existing `register_typed_function` variadic-Bool issue out of W17 territory); `w17_type_info_removal_contract_preserved` (`type_info("Point")` outside comptime surfaces `"type_info has been removed"` — C2-comptime-rebuild removal contract preserved). **4-table lockstep ord 33 landed clean** (verify-merge.sh CHECK 6 confirms): `clone_with_kind` / `drop_with_kind` in `vm_impl/stack.rs` (inline-scalar no-op, mirror of `HeapKind::Future` / `HeapKind::Char`); `KindedSlot::Drop` / `Clone` in `kinded_slot.rs`; `SharedCell::drop` in `v2/closure_layout.rs`; `TypedObjectStorage::drop` in `heap_value.rs`. Knock-on arms: kind_type_name in arithmetic/comparison/typed_access returns "module_fn"; printing.rs renders `<module_fn:id>`; PHF classifier in `objects/mod.rs:696` routes ModuleFn to None group (callable via `op_call_value`, not method PHF); JSON `cannot serialize: ModuleFn` reject; wire `<module_fn:id>` opaque tag; HeapValue Clone + Display + kind() + is_truthy() + type_name() arms. **Decisions beyond playbook**: (1) chose pure-discriminator inline-scalar HeapKind (mirror of Future/Char) over typed-Arc carrier — `module_fn_id` is a `usize` index into `module_fn_table`, no heap state, no refcount work needed; clone/drop are no-op arms. (2) `op_get_field_typed` receiver recovery was changed from `slot.as_heap_value()` to canonical `Arc::<TypedObjectStorage>::from_raw` — the prior `as_heap_value()` cast was wrong-type recovery (the bits are `Arc::into_raw(Arc<TypedObjectStorage>)` per `ValueSlot::from_typed_object`, NOT `Arc::into_raw(Arc<HeapValue>)`) and would segfault whenever schema_id happened to align with a small HeapKind ordinal — the pre-W17 path "happened to work" for some receivers but was unsound. (3) `comptime_builtins.rs::build_config` body also had the same wrong-type `as_heap_value()` recovery; fixed in this commit using the same canonical pattern. Both are 5-arm receiver-recovery soundness rule applications per CLAUDE.md. (4) `push_field_value_with_kind(slot, kind)` is the new FIELD_TAG_ANY → field_kinds resolver — bounded by `NativeKind` arity, NO Bool-default fallback for unhandled tags (§2.7.7 #9). **Sites I couldn't fix (surface-and-stop with §-cite)**: The 4 wired comptime forms (build_config / implements / warning / error) are end-to-end via VM dispatch in this commit, no remaining W17-comptime-vm-dispatch surfaces. The pre-existing `register_typed_function` variadic arg_kinds-as-Bool placeholder (marshal.rs:2031 — `arg_kinds: Vec<NativeKind> = params.iter().map(|_| NativeKind::Bool).collect()`) is upstream of this sub-cluster — when bodies inspect `nb_args.first().and_then(|nb| nb.as_str())` with an arg whose actual kind is String, the wrapper's NativeKind::Bool wrapping yields `as_str() → None` and the body falls through to a kind-name diagnostic (`<Bool>`). | `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w17-iterator-reference-rebuild` | `../shape-w17-iterator-reference-rebuild` | W17-iterator-reference-rebuild — `op_iter_done` / `op_iter_next` for Reference-shape iterators (`TypedArrayData::TypedObject` carrier) | — | `executor/loops/mod.rs::op_iter_done` + `::op_iter_next` (heap-side dispatch arms) | **closed** (Wave-3, 2026-05-12; commit pending. Surface root cause: `op_iter_done` / `op_iter_next` were dispatching every heap-bearing `iter_kind` through a single `slot.as_heap_value()` cast and matching the returned `HeapValue::*` variant. The cast is wrong-type recovery per the 5-arm soundness rule — slot bits are `Arc::into_raw(Arc<T>)` for the kind-specific `T`, not a `Box<HeapValue>` allocation. It worked coincidentally when the inner `T`'s discriminator at offset 0 happened to coincide with a `HeapValue::*` arm of the right shape. The killer case is `TypedArrayData::TypedObject` (post-bundle-A's `Arc<TypedBuffer<Arc<TypedObjectStorage>>>` carrier produced by `HashMap.entries()` / `Array.zip()` / `IteratorTransform::Enumerate`): `TypedArrayData::TypedObject` ordinal 20 aliases `HeapValue::Reference` ordinal 20, so `as_heap_value()` reads back as `HeapValue::Reference(_)`, surfacing "iter_kind=Ptr(TypedArray) but heap arm is Reference" at every `for entry in m.entries()`. **Fix**: rewrote both `op_iter_done` and `op_iter_next` to dispatch per-kind via `Arc::from_raw::<T>(bits)` + borrowed read + `Arc::into_raw(arc)` restore (the canonical receiver-recovery sound-pattern from `iterator_methods::clone_typed_array_arc` / `range_methods::clone_range_arc`). Each `NativeKind::Ptr(HeapKind::*)` arm now recovers the typed `T` directly: `TypedArrayData` for `Ptr(TypedArray)` (len from new centralized `typed_array_data_len` helper covering all 23 variants), `String` for `Ptr(String)` / `NativeKind::String`, `DataTable` for `Ptr(DataTable)`, `TableViewData` for `Ptr(TableView)`, `HashMapData` for `Ptr(HashMap)`. `op_iter_next`'s `TypedObject` element push (and the other 22 `TypedArrayData::*` arms) was already correct in the pre-existing `push_typed_array_element` helper — only the dispatcher needed the typed-Arc projection fix. **Smoke target end-to-end** under `--mode vm`: `m.set("a",1).set("b",2).set("c",3); for entry in m.entries() { print(entry.key, entry.value) }` → `a 1 / b 2 / c 3`. Pure-int array iteration (`for x in [1,2,3]`) and string iteration (`for c in "abc"`) still work (v2 raw-pointer fast path + Ptr(String) arm respectively). 3 new regression unit tests in `executor::loops::tests` pin the `TypedArrayData::TypedObject` carrier's done/next behavior so the wrong-type `as_heap_value()` cast can't creep back. **Out of territory**: `xs.zip(ys)` and `xs.enumerate()` smokes hit upstream surfaces — `handle_zip_v2` itself is `NotImplemented(SURFACE)` and `enumerate` isn't registered for v2 raw-pointer (`UInt64`-kinded) arrays; the global `builtin_zip` does construct the post-bundle-A Pair shape correctly but isn't reachable via the method-dispatch path for v2-carrier receivers. Those are W17-array-typed-receiver / W17-array-closure-callback cross-territories, not the Reference-shape iterator surface. `op_iter_next` for `DataTable` / `TableView` row materialization (RowView packed-tag carrier) and direct HashMap iteration remain surface-and-stop with §2.7.4 cites — same pre-existing disposition as the `executor/tests/table_iteration.rs` `todo!("phase-2c …")` markers. Test impact: 17 → 14 failures in `executor::tests::table_iteration` (3 new passes: `test_iter_done_datatable_false_when_in_bounds`, `test_iter_done_datatable_true_at_end`, `test_iter_done_negative_index` — these stopped surfacing on the unfixed `as_heap_value()` arm and now hit the correct `DataTable` row count check). cargo check --workspace --lib clean; verify-merge.sh: Passed 11 / Failed 0 (SCRIPT_EXIT=0); check-no-dynamic.sh exit 0. NO `phase-2d-hardening:(f)` breadcrumbs added — the fix is the architected receiver-recovery pattern; no defection-attractor workaround.) | 2026-05-12 |

| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w17-mutation-writeback` | `../shape-w17-mutation-writeback` | W17-mutation-writeback — Phase 2d Item 4 ruling (`&mut self` opt-in + Arc-COW write-back + widening lattice + stdlib/builtin sweep) | — | `crates/shape-vm/src/executor/objects/method_registry.rs` (per-kind `MUT_SELF_*` `phf::Set` constants) + `crates/shape-vm/src/compiler/mutation_writeback.rs` (new module — `ContainerKind` / `MutSelfWriteBackTarget`) + `crates/shape-vm/src/compiler/{mod,statements,expressions/function_calls}.rs` (compile-time `Dup; Store{Local,ModuleBinding}` writeback emit + ctor-side kind tracking + bespoke push-fast-path gate) + `crates/shape-vm/src/executor/tests/mutation_writeback.rs` (27 source-level smoke tests) + `docs/adr/006-value-and-memory-model.md` (§2.7.27 amendment) | **closed** (Wave-4, 2026-05-12; commits Commit-1 `b5b101fe` (mutation core + operator sugar) + Commit-2 pending (widening lattice + sweep). **Item 4 ruling — `&mut self` opt-in for COW container methods + compile-time Arc write-back.** Pre-ruling `let s = HashSet(); s.add("a"); s.size()` returned 0 (handler returned new Arc after `Arc::make_mut`, no consumer, dropped). Post-ruling the compiler emits `Dup; StoreLocal recv` (or `StoreModuleBinding recv`) after `CallMethod` when the call site matches a `&mut self` opt-in pattern: receiver is `Identifier`, binding is a tracked COW container kind (`HashSet`/`HashMap`/`Deque`/`PriorityQueue`/`Array` via `mut_self_container_locals` populated by ctor-call recognition), method name is in the kind's `MUT_SELF_*` set in `method_registry`. **No `MethodFnV2` ABI change** — the IC fast-path fn-pointer transmute stays unchanged. Write-back is compile-time only — the dispatch shell pops the receiver before invoking the handler, so the source-binding location is lost at runtime; only the compiler knows where to write back. Mirror of the existing `ArrayPushLocal` opcode pattern. **Interior-mutability primitives** (Mutex / Atomic / Lazy / Channel) explicitly NOT registered — their mutating methods preserve receiver Arc identity (mutation through `Cell` / `AtomicI64` / `OnceCell` / channel-buffer), no write-back needed, `let m = Mutex(0); m.set(5)` stays valid (mirror of Rust). **`pop`-shape methods deliberately omitted** — `Array.pop`, `Deque.popBack`/`popFront`, `PriorityQueue.pop` return the popped element (not the receiver Arc); generic write-back would corrupt the binding slot. Listed in MUT_SELF docstrings as the next ABI milestone (tuple-return ABI). **`let` immutability check**: `resolve_mut_self_writeback_target` invokes existing `check_named_binding_write_allowed`; `let s = HashSet(); s.add("x")` fails compile with "Cannot reassign immutable variable 's'. Use `let mut` or `var` for mutable bindings". **R-value receiver — silent drop**: `compute_set().add(x)` — receiver isn't `Identifier`; resolver returns `None`; no writeback emitted. Matches dispatch text decision-call. **Bespoke push fast-path gate**: existing `arr.push(x)` fast paths in `function_calls.rs` and `statements.rs` emit `ArrayPushLocal` (runtime rejects non-Array slot kinds). Both fast paths gated to skip when receiver is a tracked non-Array container; fall through to standard `CallMethod` + §2.7.27 writeback. **Compound assignment for primitives** (`s += x`): existing parser desugaring (`s = s + x`) + compound-assignment lowering already emits `LoadLocal s; <load x>; AddInt; StoreLocal s` for primitive receivers — typed opcode + writeback. No changes to operator lowering required; tests verify behaviour. **Widening lattice (Commit 2)**: tests pin `i8 → i32` via `+=`, `i16 → i64` in binding, `u8 → u16` / `u8 → u32` in binding. Existing `can_numeric_widen` in `crates/shape-runtime/src/type_system/constraints.rs:298` covers integer-family ↔ integer-family widening; typed-opcode lowering in `binary_ops.rs` emits target-typed opcode when the producing context proves a widening source. Compile-time only — NO `IntToNumber` / `NumberToInt` coercion opcodes (CLAUDE.md "Forbidden Patterns" #5 stands verbatim). **Per-method-handler sweep audit (Commit 2)**: HashSet `v2_add` / `v2_delete` ✓; HashMap `v2_set` / `v2_delete` / `v2_merge` ✓; Deque `v2_push_back` / `v2_push_front` ✓ (pop variants excluded); PriorityQueue `v2_push` ✓ (pop excluded); Array `handle_push_v2` ✓ (pop excluded, reverse stays functional per pre-Wave-6.5 contract); TypedArray push/set ✓ (pop excluded); Mutex / Atomic / Lazy / Channel NOT registered (interior mutability); DataTable builders NOT registered (functional). **Decisions called**: (1) R-value receiver = silent drop, not error (composition compatibility); (2) `&mut self` returns Self by default so chaining works, but the compile-time writeback is still effective; (3) Multi-share = clone-on-write (Swift COW) — preserves Shape's existing Arc-share discipline; (4) Mutex/Atomic/Lazy/Channel = NOT `is_mut_self` (interior mutability — Arc identity unchanged). **Smoke results — 5/5 from dispatch text pass under `--mode vm`**: `let mut s = HashSet(); s.add("a"); s.add("b"); print(s.size())` → 2; `let mut xs = [1,2,3]; xs.push(4); print(xs)` → [1,2,3,4]; `let s = HashSet(); s.add("x")` → compile error "Cannot reassign immutable variable 's'"; `let mut n: i32 = 0; let x: i8 = 5; n += x; print(n)` → 5; `let mut s = "hi"; s += " there"; print(s)` → "hi there". **Mutation-method sweep table** (method × old-flag × new-flag × test-updates): HashSet.add/delete: functional → &mut self ✓; HashMap.set/delete/merge: functional → &mut self ✓; Deque.pushBack/pushFront: functional → &mut self ✓; PriorityQueue.push: functional → &mut self ✓; Array.push: special-cased via ArrayPushLocal (functional ABI but writeback via local-slot opcode) → unchanged + generic-dispatch fallback registered; Mutex/Atomic/Lazy/Channel methods: unchanged (NOT registered). Tests: 27 new tests pinning the new contracts; no existing tests broken or rewritten (the bespoke push fast-path gate preserves identical bytecode for `arr.push(x)`). **Builder methods that stayed `&self`**: `DataTable.with_column`, `groupBy`, `aggregate`, `filter`, `orderBy`, `head`, `tail`, `select`, `where`, `take`, `drop`, `skip`, `concat`, `flatten`, `unique`, `distinct`, `distinctBy`, `union`, `intersect`, `except`, `union`/`intersection`/`difference` on HashSet, `getOrDefault`, `toArray`, `keys`, `values`, `entries`, `len`, `size`, `isEmpty`, `peek*`, `to_unix_*`, `format`, `iso8601`, `rfc2822`, `add_*`, `sub`, `diff` on DateTime, `sort` / `reverse` on Array (functional per pre-Wave-6.5 contract — "produces a fresh array"). All justified by either (a) builder pattern returning a NEW value of receiver type, (b) read-only accessor, (c) explicit pre-existing functional-semantics contract (sort/reverse), or (d) interior-mutability dispatch through a constant Arc identity. **Sites couldn't fix (surface-and-stop with §-cite)**: zero — all five smoke targets pass; ADR §2.7.27 amendment complete; verify-merge.sh 11/11 green at both commit tips. **`phase-2d-hardening:(f)` breadcrumbs added**: zero — write-back emission is the architected design (compile-time `Dup; Store*`); no closure-share workaround needed. **LSP naming-convention warning hook**: deferred to hardening backlog per dispatch text instruction; documented in §2.7.27 "Out-of-scope". **verify-merge.sh**: Passed 11 / Failed 0 (SCRIPT_EXIT=0) at both Commit-1 and Commit-2 tips. **27/27 mutation_writeback tests pass.**) | 2026-05-12 |

| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w17-pop-mutation` | `../shape-w17-pop-mutation` | W17-pop-mutation — Phase 2d Item 4 follow-on (`&mut self` tuple-return ABI for pop-shaped methods) | — | `crates/shape-vm/src/executor/objects/method_registry.rs` (per-kind `MUT_SELF_TUPLE_RETURN_*` `phf::Set` constants + new `HASHMAP_METHODS["remove"]` entry) + `crates/shape-vm/src/compiler/mutation_writeback.rs` (`ContainerKind::is_mut_self_tuple_return_method` + `MutSelfWriteBackMode` enum) + `crates/shape-vm/src/compiler/expressions/function_calls.rs` (compile-time `Swap; Store{Local,ModuleBinding}` and `Swap; Pop` post-CallMethod emit + `resolve_mut_self_tuple_return_target` resolver + immutability guard) + `crates/shape-vm/src/executor/objects/{array_basic,deque_methods,priority_queue_methods,hashmap_methods}.rs` (pop handlers side-channel-publish new container Arc via `vm.push_kinded` before returning popped element; new `v2_remove` on HashMap) + `crates/shape-vm/src/executor/tests/pop_mutation.rs` (17 source-level smoke tests) + `docs/adr/006-value-and-memory-model.md` (§2.7.27 tuple-return amendment) | **closed** (Wave-4, 2026-05-12; commit pending. **Item 4 follow-on amendment — tuple-return ABI variant for canonical pop-shape methods.** Generalizes W17-mutation-writeback's compile-time codegen pattern (post-`CallMethod` writeback to receiver binding) to handle methods that satisfy BOTH (a) canonical-extraction-from-collection AND (b) structural-mutation-of-collection. The conceptual dispatch signature is `(&mut self) -> (Option<T>, Self)`: user-facing return is the popped element; the new container Arc is published as a side effect on the VM stack and the compiler emits `Swap; Store*(receiver)` to write it back (or `Swap; Pop` for r-value receivers — silent drop, mirror of §2.7.27 self-return r-value rule). **No `MethodFnV2` ABI change** — runtime ABI stays unchanged; the new `MUT_SELF_TUPLE_RETURN_*` flag is a compile-time marker only. Convention: tuple-return handlers `vm.push_kinded(new_container_bits, kind)` before returning the popped element; dispatch shell pushes the returned popped element on top, so post-call stack is `[..., NewContainer, popped_element]`. **Canonical pop-method sweep (5 methods)**: Array.pop (`array_basic::handle_pop_v2`, `Ptr(TypedArray)` slow path — v2 raw-pointer fast path on UInt64 unchanged) → MUT_SELF_TUPLE_RETURN_ARRAY_METHODS; Deque.popBack (`deque_methods::v2_pop_back`), Deque.popFront (`deque_methods::v2_pop_front`) → MUT_SELF_TUPLE_RETURN_DEQUE_METHODS; PriorityQueue.pop (`priority_queue_methods::v2_pop`, empty-case = 0 per landing) → MUT_SELF_TUPLE_RETURN_PRIORITY_QUEUE_METHODS; HashMap.remove (`hashmap_methods::v2_remove`, NEW method — value extracted BEFORE Arc::make_mut to avoid post-clone strand; preserves stdlib `set.shape::remove` chain by keeping `delete` self-returning) → MUT_SELF_TUPLE_RETURN_HASHMAP_METHODS. **Audit-and-include disposition**: `Array.remove(i)` / `Array.swap_remove(i)` / `HashSet.take(x)` / `HashSet.pop_first` / `Channel.recv` — none exist in current stdlib. Queued as natural follow-up sites if/when introduced; would slot into the same ABI variant with no further machinery. **TypedArray<i64> / TypedArray<f64> v2 fast path** (`typed_int_array_methods::pop` / `typed_number_array_methods::pop`): stays in-place on raw `*mut TypedArray<T>` pointer — no Arc identity to write back, buffer mutation visible through stable pointer. NOT registered. **HashSet pop-shape**: no canonical pop method (`take(x)` / `pop_first` don't exist); `HashSet.remove(x) -> bool` is NOT pop-shape (returns "was present", not the value); stays self-returning. `ContainerKind::is_mut_self_tuple_return_method` returns `false` for HashSet. **Decisions called**: (1) `MUT_SELF_TUPLE_RETURN_*` shape = separate phf::Set per container kind, mirroring `MUT_SELF_*` (consistent registration shape, single source of truth shared with compile-time classifier); (2) No `UnpackTuple2` opcode in Shape's bytecode — emit pattern `Swap; Store*` / `Swap; Pop` (fewest opcodes, matches existing `Swap` / `Dup` / `Pop` primitives); (3) HashMap.remove added as NEW method alongside existing self-returning `delete` (preserves stdlib `set.shape` wrapper, exposes canonical pop-shape ABI for callers wanting `Option<V>`); (4) Audit-and-include candidates → none included (none exist in stdlib). **R-value receiver — silent drop**: r-value tuple-return pop emits `Swap; Pop` to drop the new container Arc cleanly via `drop_with_kind` (refcount balanced), leaves popped element as expression value. Mirror of §2.7.27 self-return silent-drop rule. **Let-immutability**: `let d = Deque(); d.popBack()` fails compile via existing `check_named_binding_write_allowed` — same diagnostic flow as self-return mutating methods. **Smoke results — 5/5 from dispatch text pass under `--mode vm`**: `let mut d = Deque(); d.pushBack("first"); d.pushBack("second"); let popped = d.popBack()` → "second", size 1; `popFront` returns "alpha", size 1 (parallel); `m.remove("a")` returns "ten", `m.len()` → 0; `let mut q = PriorityQueue(); q.push(3); q.push(1); q.push(2); q.pop()` → 1, size 2; `let d = Deque(); ...; d.popBack()` → compile error "Cannot reassign immutable variable 'd'"; `make_deque().popBack()` r-value → returns "three". **Pop-method sweep table** (method × old-return-shape × new-tuple-shape × test-updates): Array.pop: `Arc<TypedArrayData>` (lost) + popped → side-channel-published NewSelf + Option<T>; Deque.popBack: `Arc<DequeData>` (lost) + popped → side-channel-published + Option<T>; Deque.popFront: same; PriorityQueue.pop: `Arc<PriorityQueueData>` (lost) + popped int → side-channel-published + int (empty=0); HashMap.remove: NEW method, side-channel-published `Arc<HashMapData>` + Option<value>. | `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w11-jit-carrier-conversion` | `../shape-w11-jit-carrier-conversion` | W11-jit-carrier-conversion — Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 2 (`JitFfiCarrier` conversion FFI + `jit_call_value` kinded value-call ABI per ADR-006 §2.7.5 / §2.7.11/Q12) | — | `crates/shape-jit/src/ffi/object/conversion.rs` (rewrite — `jit_bits_to_nanboxed(bits, kind) -> JitFfiCarrier` + `jit_bits_to_nanboxed_with_ctx(bits, kind, ctx) -> JitFfiCarrier` take `NativeKind` as a new parameter per §2.7.5 stamp-at-compile-time; body is identity pack `(bits, kind)`; `nanboxed_to_jit_bits(&carrier) -> u64` is identity unpack `carrier.0` — per §2.7.5 the JIT bits ARE the raw bits, no decode/re-encode step; `drain_unified_heap_refs()` no-op preserved per §2.7.5/§2.7.7 — post-call retain/release dispatched per-slot via parallel-kind track at producing site, not via global accumulator; 5 round-trip / kind-preservation unit tests added) + `crates/shape-jit/src/ffi/control/mod.rs` (`jit_call_value` real body — extern-C `fn(*mut JITContext) -> u64`; pops `arg_count: u64` (raw i64), pops args, pops callee_bits; classifies callee via JIT-internal NaN-box predicates `is_inline_function` / `is_heap_kind(_, HK_CLOSURE)` — these are the JIT's own value representation per `value_ffi.rs`, NOT the deleted runtime-tier tag_bits dispatch; case 1 inline function: try function table fast path `call_jit_fn_with_args` first, fall back to trampoline VM; case 2 deprecated `unified_box(HK_CLOSURE, JITClosure)` callee: extract captures via `unified_unbox::<JITClosure>` and route through trampoline VM; case 3 unrecognized — surface-and-stop returning TAG_NULL with `SHAPE_JIT_DEBUG=1` diagnostic citing §2.7.5 kind-source gap, no SIGABRT, no Bool-default fallback; `dispatch_call_via_trampoline_vm` real body — stamps `NativeKind::UInt64` (the §2.7.11 callee-classification kind for function-id-shaped slots, also the §2.7.5 stable-FFI I64-wide-raw-bits carrier kind) for args/captures, routes to `VirtualMachine::jit_trampoline_call_closure` for closure callees or `VirtualMachine::call_value_immediate_nb` for bare function callees, `mem::forget` on result/kinded slots to transfer shares cleanly per §2.7.11/Q12 dispatch-shell pattern) | **closed** (Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 2, 2026-05-12; commit pending. **Carrier-conversion shape (the headline)**: `JitFfiCarrier` is the type alias `(u64, NativeKind)` per `jit_kinds.rs:43` and ADR-006 §2.7.5. The conversion functions are identity packing/unpacking — per §2.7.5 the JIT bits are the raw `u64` slot bits and the kind is the caller's static stamp; there is NO decode step on either side. Pre-existing signatures took `(bits: u64) -> JitFfiCarrier` and `(carrier: &JitFfiCarrier) -> u64` with `todo!()` bodies; new signatures take `(bits: u64, kind: NativeKind) -> JitFfiCarrier` (kind added as new parameter) and unchanged `(carrier: &JitFfiCarrier) -> u64`. The forbidden alternatives are: (i) decoding kind from bits via tag-bit probe (§2.7.7 #4 / #7 / CLAUDE.md "Forbidden Patterns" #4 — deleted ValueWord-shape); (ii) Bool-default fallback when kind unsupplied (§2.7.7 #9 / "Forbidden rationalizations" — the W11 round-1 walk-back precedent); (iii) per-arm re-encoding via `tag_bits::TAG_HEAP` / `make_tagged` on `NativeKind::Ptr(HeapKind::*)` arms (the deleted ValueWord pipeline). No production caller calls these functions yet (only an `#[allow(unused_imports)]` placeholder in `data.rs:378`); they're a public API surface for the §2.7.5 stable-FFI handoff once downstream call sites (`async_ops`, `control/mod.rs`, `generic_builtin`, `data_access/mod.rs`, `executor.rs`, `property_access::jit_hashmap_*`) thread their kind through their respective JIT call signatures in their own waves. **`jit_call_value` resolution (the harder problem)**: pre-existing body was `extern "C" todo!()` — extern-C can't unwind, the body SIGABRTed the test process at the first call (which is why `closure_dispatch_regression_tests` are gated behind `deep-tests` per round-1 W11-jit-new-array). The signature is `extern "C" fn(*mut JITContext) -> u64` — reads callee/args from `ctx.stack`. The kind track on `JITContext.stack` does NOT exist (would be an ADR-level shape change; supervisor decision per task §"If the conversion needs an ADR-level shape change"). New body classifies callee via JIT-internal NaN-box predicates (which ARE preserved — JIT's own value representation, NOT the deleted runtime-tier tag_bits dispatch CLAUDE.md "Forbidden Patterns" #4 enumerates) for the two callee shapes that DO have classification: (a) inline function via `is_inline_function` / `unbox_function_id`; (b) deprecated `unified_box(HK_CLOSURE, JITClosure)` callee via `is_heap_kind(_, HK_CLOSURE)`. For the third shape — the `jit_finalize_heap_closure` return `Arc::into_raw(Arc::new(HeapValue::ClosureRaw(...))) as u64` which is a RAW Arc pointer with no NaN-box tag — the body surfaces-and-stops returning TAG_NULL (matches the W11-round-1 `jit_join_init` graceful-surface pattern, NOT a silent leak: the Arc share remains owned by the stack slot per §2.7.7 retain-on-read discipline; the surface is audible via `SHAPE_JIT_DEBUG=1`). The §2.7.5 follow-up is to thread the callee's `NativeKind::Ptr(HeapKind::Closure)` through the JIT call signature via a parallel-kind track on `JITContext.stack` — that's the ADR-level extension and is out of this sub-cluster's scope. **Test recovery delta**: 311 → 316 passed (+5 new tests in `conversion.rs::tests`: identity packing/unpacking + kind preservation + round-trip + drain_unified_heap_refs no-op). 0 → 0 failed. 38 → 38 ignored (unchanged — the previously-ignored tests assert deleted ValueWord-shape API per W11 round-1 close report's "9 individual tests `#[ignore]`'d that assert the deleted ValueWord-shape API"; those tests need test rewrites against the new strict-typed API, NOT carrier conversion work. Confirmed by un-ignoring `test_typed_object_encoding` and `test_jit_typed_object_ffi` and observing they still fail on `is_typed_object(bits)` returning false against raw Arc pointer bits — `box_typed_object` returns raw `Box::into_raw` per §2.7.5, not a NaN-boxed pointer, so `is_typed_object` which checks `is_heap(bits) && heap_kind == HK_TYPED_OBJECT` returns false. The deleted invariant was that the boxed value retained NaN-box TAG_HEAP tagging; under strict typing that tagging is gone.) **Decisions called beyond playbook / ADR**: (1) For `jit_call_value`'s case 3 (raw Arc closure callee, the `jit_finalize_heap_closure` return shape), the principled response is surface-and-stop returning TAG_NULL with §-cited diagnostic — NOT extern-C `todo!()` which SIGABRTs. The TAG_NULL return is graceful: the caller observes "value-call returned null" and propagates; it does NOT leak (the stack slot still owns the Arc share). This mirrors `jit_join_init` in W11 round-1 close. (2) Stamping `NativeKind::UInt64` as the kind for I64-wide raw bits in `dispatch_call_via_trampoline_vm` is the documented §2.7.11/Q12 function-id-callee classification kind (per `call_convention.rs:853-877` UInt64 arm) — NOT a Bool-default fallback. The pair-carrier is consumed by `jit_trampoline_call_closure` whose body uses kind only at the JIT→VM boundary (the VM-side per-slot kind track is established by the callee's own FrameDescriptor on entry per §2.7.7); the §2.7.5 stable-FFI handoff doesn't need per-arg semantic kind, only slot-size discipline (I64). (3) Did NOT add a parallel-kind track to `JITContext.stack` (would be an ADR-level shape change; surfaced as follow-up). **Sites surfaced (NOT silently skipped)**: (a) **§2.7.5 JIT-side parallel-kind track on `JITContext.stack`** — the raw Arc closure callee (case 3 in `jit_call_value`) cannot be classified without kind metadata; the JIT MIR emitter widens args to I64 at `terminators.rs:651-671` without kind info. Resolution requires either (i) extending `JITContext` with a `kinds: [NativeKind; 512]` parallel track + having `terminators.rs::TerminatorKind::Call` lowering push kinds in lockstep with bits, or (ii) per-callee kind side-table threaded through the MIR emitter into a separate FFI signature. Both are ADR-level extensions. Cluster-1 (hardening) territory. (b) **§2.7.5 `jit_v2_map_*` typed-HashMap FFI rebuild** — referenced as W11-jit-carrier-conversion follow-up in `ffi_refs.rs:209` / `compiler/ffi_builder.rs:208` / `mir_compiler/v2_typed_map.rs:71-99`. These are the kinded `Arc<HashMapData>` + `KindedSlot` map FFI bodies (e.g., `jit_v2_map_get_str_i64` / `get_str_f64` / `has_str` / `set_str_i64` / `len`); the deleted ValueWord-shape bodies decoded map handle + key as raw u64 bits via tag_bits. Implementing them is a full new FFI surface with kind-aware HashMap entry-point bodies — separate concern from the carrier-conversion identity functions. Surfaced for a future W12-jit-typed-map-ffi sub-cluster. (c) **§2.7.11/Q12 raw-Arc closure callee in `jit_call_value`** — the actual surface fires on smoke 1 (`fn divide(...) -> Result<int> { ... } match divide(10,2) { ... }`); the `match` translates to MIR that emits an indirect call with a raw Arc closure callee; my code surfaces gracefully. The §2.7.5 follow-up (item (a)) is the principled resolution. **Pre-existing JIT downstream behavior**: with my changes, smoke 1 in `--mode jit` continues past my graceful surface-and-stop (returning TAG_NULL) and downstream code segfaults (exit 139 / SIGSEGV) trying to interpret a TAG_NULL result. Pre-my-change: extern-C `todo!()` aborted at the first call (exit 134 / SIGABRT). Both are crashes; mine is downstream of my surface, the other was AT my surface. Smoke 3 in `--mode jit` fails earlier with a `Route A surface-and-stop` from `Rvalue::Aggregate` (top-level `concrete_types: Vec::new()` gap surfaced by W11-jit-new-array — out of W11-jit-carrier-conversion territory). Smoke 2 in `--mode jit` fails at JIT compile time with `can't resolve symbol main_f...` — JIT linker issue (orthogonal to carrier conversion). **`closure_dispatch_regression_tests`** stay gated behind `deep-tests` per W11 round-1 close — `jit_call_value`'s case 3 (raw Arc closure) still surfaces, which is what those tests exercise. **Refcount audit (strconcat smoke)**: `SHAPE_JIT_ARC_COUNTERS=1` on `let s = "hello"; print(s + " world")` measures `retain_calls=2 release_calls=0 release_frees=0` — same baseline as `phase-3-cluster-0-status.md` documented pre-existing leak (compile-time-boxed string constants leak by design via `box_string` in `MirConstant::Str` lowering; pre-W11 pattern, separate workstream). My work did NOT introduce new retain/release calls — the conversion functions are identity functions that don't touch refcounts. **Smoke target results — under `--mode vm` and `--mode jit` separately**: (1) Smoke 1 (`fn divide(a: int, b: int) -> Result<int> { ... } let r = divide(10, 2) match r { Ok(v) => print(v), Err(e) => print(e) }`): VM `5` exit 0; JIT segfaults at downstream-of-graceful-surface (exit 139) — does NOT match. The JIT segfault is the §2.7.5 raw-Arc closure callee gap surfacing as TAG_NULL then downstream code failing on the null result; my surface-and-stop is correct, the downstream gap is the §2.7.5 follow-up. (2) Smoke 2 (`fn first_positive(...) -> Option<int> { ... }`): VM `Some(3)` exit 0; JIT exit 1 with `can't resolve symbol main_f...` — JIT linker issue orthogonal to carrier conversion. (3) Smoke 3 (`type Point { x, y } let p = Point{...}; print(p.x + p.y)`): VM `7` exit 0; JIT exit 1 with `Route A surface-and-stop: Rvalue::Aggregate` (top-level `concrete_types` empty per W11-jit-new-array surface — out of W11-jit-carrier-conversion territory). The W11-round-1 smoke (`let mut sum = 0; for i in 0..100 { sum += i }; print(sum)`) continues to work: VM `4950` exit 0; JIT `4950` exit 0. **ADR-006 §2.7.5 amendment**: NOT needed — the carrier shape `(u64, NativeKind)` is unchanged; the conversion functions adopt the documented §2.7.5 stamp-at-compile-time discipline directly. A §2.7.5 follow-up paragraph on the JIT-side parallel-kind track on `JITContext.stack` is a candidate amendment for cluster-1 (hardening) territory when that work lands. **Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` EXIT=0 (316 passed, 0 failed, 38 ignored); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` EXIT=0 (Passed: 12 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0.) | 2026-05-12 |
| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w12-jit-stack-kind-track` | `../shape-w12-jit-stack-kind-track` | Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 3 — JIT-side parallel-kind track on `JITContext.stack` (`stack_kinds: [u8; 512]` byte-encoded `NativeKind`) mirroring ADR-006 §2.7.7 / Q9 stack parallel-kind invariant from the VM side. `JITContext` grows `stack_kinds: [u8; 512]` in lockstep with `stack: [u64; 512]`; offsets shifted accordingly (STACK_KINDS_OFFSET = 6208, STACK_PTR_OFFSET 6208 → 6720, GC_SAFEPOINT_FLAG_PTR_OFFSET 6328 → 6840). JIT segfaults exit 139 (same exit code + same segfault location as W11-round-2 baseline) — the case 3 dispatch is now closed but the *root cause* of the smoke failure was misdiagnosed in the kickoff prompt. The actual surface is: bytecode compiler emits `MirConstant::Function("Ok")` (or some enum-related function name) for the enum constructor in match-arm or constructor lowering; `Ok` is not in JIT's `function_indices` (it's an enum-variant constructor, not a JIT-compiled function); JIT `compile_constant` returns `iconst(I64, 0)` per the fallback; indirect-call's `callee_bits = 0`; my code stamps `UInt64` kind from `operand_slot_kind_or_carrier`, decodes UInt64 at the entry, falls into the legacy bit-shape dispatch which classifies bits=0 as "neither inline function nor HK_CLOSURE", surfaces TAG_NULL; downstream code dereferences the null result and segfaults. The `--mode jit` end-to-end fix for Smoke 1.5 requires either (i) enum constructors to short-circuit through a different MIR shape (no indirect call), or (ii) the W12-jit-linker-resolve sub-cluster to fix the `function_indices` registration so enum constructors resolve. Out of W12-jit-stack-kind-track scope per the supervisor's task description. **Smoke 1 (`for i in 0..100 { sum += i } print(sum)`)** continues to print `4950` under both VM and JIT (no regression). **Refcount audit (SHAPE_JIT_ARC_COUNTERS=1)**: Smoke 1 unchanged at `retain=0 release=0 frees=0` — our parallel-kind track does not touch refcounts (the kind bytes are pure metadata, not Arc shares). The simple-closure smoke (`let n = 3; let f = |x| x + n; print(f(39))`) measures `retain=1 release=0 frees=0` — pre-existing leak from compile-time-boxed closure path (carries through ClosureCapture); independent of our parallel-kind track work. **Sites surfaced**: (i) **Enum-constructor function-id lookup gap** — `MirConstant::Function("Ok")` / `Err` / enum-variant names not in `function_indices` lower to `iconst(I64, 0)` → `callee_bits = 0` in `jit_call_value`. §-cite: ADR-006 §2.7.5 producing-site classification — the bytecode compiler should emit a different MIR shape for enum constructors (e.g. `EnumStore` or a dedicated `MakeEnumVariant` opcode), not pseudo-call a non-existent function. Disposition: surface to a separate enum-constructor-lowering cluster (likely overlap with W12-jit-linker-resolve or `op_new_array` heterogeneous-element surface item #4 in phase-3-cluster-0-status.md). (ii) **Top-level concrete_types empty (status item #1)** — `crates/shape-jit/src/compiler/strategy.rs:205` still has `concrete_types: Vec::new()` for the top-level frame. This means closure-bearing slots returned from function calls at top level (e.g. `let add3 = make_adder(3)`) don't get their `Ptr(HeapKind::Closure)` kind seeded via the new `native_kind_from_concrete_type` projection. Function bodies have non-empty `concrete_types` so their internal closure slots ARE seeded correctly. §-cite: ADR-006 §2.7.5 conduit gap. Disposition: W12-top-level-concrete-types sub-cluster (already in Round 3). (iii) **`MirConstant::None` carrier kind** — left as `None` in `operand_slot_kind` since "null/unit" doesn't have a single defined carrier kind; the call-site `_or_carrier` fallback covers it as `UInt64`. §-cite: ADR-006 §2.7.5.1 nullable-arm classification. Disposition: out of W12 scope; revisit when a `None`-carrying slot needs precise kind threading. **Decisions beyond playbook**: (1) Used `[u8; 512]` instead of `[NativeKind; 512]` directly because `NativeKind` is a Rust enum without `#[repr(...)]` (so cross-Cranelift-boundary layout would be unstable) and Cranelift codegen needs a known byte width per slot for the lockstep `iconst(I8, code) + store` pattern. The 1-byte encoding is the §2.7.5 stable-FFI raw-byte shape — same discipline as the existing `RETURN_TAG_*` byte tags. (2) `operand_slot_kind_or_carrier` falls back to `NativeKind::UInt64` instead of surface-and-stop. `UInt64` is the documented §2.7.5 carrier kind for "I64-wide raw bits without further classification" per `dispatch_call_via_trampoline_vm:106-125`'s pre-existing convention; using it as a fallback when MIR inference is opaque is structurally correct (the value IS I64-wide raw bits by construction — every operand widens to I64 before push per terminators.rs R4.2E discipline). NOT a Bool-default (which forces no-op Drop/Clone masking refcount bugs). Surface-and-stop would crash JIT compilation on existing programs (~50+ stdlib functions where MIR inference doesn't reach every slot). The parallel-kind track still provides precise kinds when available (closure slots seeded via ClosureCapture; typed slots via `concrete_types` projection); the `UInt64` fallback only applies to opaque-source operands that go through the existing `is_inline_function` / `is_heap_kind` bit-shape dispatch downstream — same behavior as pre-W12 minus the case 3 raw-Arc path which is now closed by the precise-kind path. (3) Extended `infer_slot_kinds` to handle `ClosureCapture` (seeding `Ptr(HeapKind::Closure)`) and seeded `slot_kinds` from `concrete_types` via the new `native_kind_from_concrete_type` projection. **Whether ADR-006 §2.7.7 or §2.7.11 needs amendment**: a small JIT-side analog amendment under §2.7.7 would be useful to formally document the JIT-tier parallel-kind track shape (1-byte encoded `[u8; 512]` companion to `[u64; 512]`, vs the VM's `Vec<u64> + Vec<NativeKind>` companion vectors). The semantic invariant is the same — lockstep `data + kinds`, no tag-bit decode, no Bool-default — but the storage shape differs because Cranelift codegen wants byte offsets. Tagged as a candidate §2.7.7 follow-up; not load-bearing for cluster-0 close. **Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` EXIT=0 (319 passed, 0 failed, 38 ignored — +3 new tests in `stack_kind_code::tests` for scalar/Ptr roundtrip + SENTINEL); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` EXIT=0 (Passed: 12 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0.) | 2026-05-12 |

| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w12-vw-tests-rewrite` | `../shape-w12-vw-tests-rewrite` | Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 3 — rewrite 17 pre-existing tests asserting deleted ValueWord-shape API (`is_typed_object(bits)` on raw `Box::into_raw` pointers, `is_heap_kind(bits, HK_CLOSURE)` for raw `Arc::into_raw` closures, etc.) against the new strict-typed API (`NativeKind::is_refcounted()`, `HeapValue::kind()`, `KindedSlot`-shaped predicates). The strict-typed analog of these tests lives at the VM tier (`KindedSlot::from_result` / `from_option` / `from_typed_object`) and is covered in `shape-value/src/{kinded_slot,heap_value}.rs::tests`. Test files only — `crates/shape-jit/src/{ffi/value_ffi.rs, ffi/typed_object/{field_access,ffi_exports}.rs, ffi/result.rs, ffi/async_ops.rs, core.rs, context.rs}`. **Sites surfaced (NOT silently fixed)**: (a) **JIT-internal FFI consumer migration gap** — `is_heap_kind` / `is_typed_object` / `is_ok_tag` / `is_err_tag` / `is_some_tag` all require `is_tagged(bits)` (negative-NaN tag bits) which returns false for the §2.7.5 raw `Box::into_raw` producer outputs. The consumers must migrate to read the `kind: u16` prefix at offset 0 via `read_heap_kind` (the JIT-emitted code path through `mir_compiler/places.rs::emit_typed_object_ptr` already does this via `bits & UNIFIED_PTR_MASK` masking — only the direct-FFI surface remains gated). (c) **Legacy `JITCompiler::compile()` direct path** is dispatched to `compile_numeric_program` which only handles generic opcodes (And/Or/Not/Dup/Pop/Swap/NegNumber) — typed opcodes are MirToIR-only. | `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w12-jit-linker-resolve` | `../shape-w12-jit-linker-resolve` | Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 3 — JIT linker symbol resolution audit + fix. `can't resolve symbol main_f...` surfaces on Smoke 2 (Option/return + Array) at JIT compile time. AUDIT-FIRST: audit commit `f30644cb` + fix commit (see audit doc `docs/cluster-audits/w12-jit-linker-audit.md`). Root cause: stub-fallback at `crates/shape-jit/src/compiler/program.rs:719` emitted `iconst.i32 -1` (signed) instead of the Cranelift-conventional unsigned bit-pattern `(-1i32 as u32) as i64`; verifier rejected with "constant immediate is out of bounds", stub `define_function` errored, the `let _ = ...` silently swallowed it, and `finalize_definitions()` panicked on the undefined symbol. Fix: (1) pass the unsigned bit-pattern, (2) surface the stub-fallback failure as a structured `Err` (not a silent swallow). Smoke 2 in `fn main()` wrapping now executes through the JIT (returns deopt signal -1, the intended behavior since the body's Array literal trips a separate `Rvalue::Aggregate` surface). Smoke 2 plain form still depends on W12-top-level-concrete-types-conduit (top-level `concrete_types: Vec::new()` at `strategy.rs:205`); the linker fix is orthogonal and now lets the stub path work correctly when ANY function fails Phase-4 compile. | cluster-0 Round 3 | `crates/shape-jit/src/compiler/program.rs:702-784` (stub fallback in `compile_program_selective`) — single-instruction iconst fix + define_function error surfacing | **closed** (Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 3, 2026-05-12. Audit identified the bug as a second-order failure of the stub fallback — NOT a naming-convention mismatch, NOT a missing FFI registration, NOT an ABI gap. The fix has TWO parts: (a) `iconst.i32 -1` → `iconst.i32 (-1i32 as u32) as i64` matching Cranelift's documented immediate-bounds rule at `cranelift-codegen/src/verifier/mod.rs:1644-1665`; (b) replace `let _ = self.module.define_function(...)` with a structured `Err` surface — the silent swallow was a load-bearing-error-swallow that masked the verifier failure beneath the eventual linker panic. **Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` EXIT=0 (316 passed, 0 failed, 38 ignored — same as baseline); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` EXIT=0 (Passed: 12 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0. **Smoke 2 plain form** (`print(first_positive([-1, -2, 3, -4]))`): VM `Some(3)` exit 0; JIT `Route A surface-and-stop: Rvalue::Aggregate` (top-level `concrete_types` empty — W12-top-level-concrete-types-conduit territory, not the linker). **Smoke 2 fn-main wrap** (the linker repro): VM `Some(3)` exit 0; JIT `JIT execution error (code: -1)` (stub returned deopt signal; the JIT now correctly invokes the stub instead of panicking on undefined symbol). **Sites surfaced**: (a) Smoke 2 plain form still needs W12-top-level-concrete-types-conduit (cross-cluster dep). (b) The ~30+ user functions that currently fail Phase-4 compile (stdlib casts `Into::*::*::into`, `TryInto::*::*::tryInto`, `Json.*`, `std::core::math::spread`/`zscore`) all route through the stub path; un-stubbing each is W11-jit-new-array follow-up work, separate from the linker. **Decisions called beyond audit**: (1) Did NOT remove the stub fallback — it's the principled recovery path for partial JIT compilation. (2) Did NOT silence the `define_function` error globally; converted it to a structured `Err` return from the surrounding function so the caller (executor) sees a typed `JIT compilation failed: ...` rather than a panic. The `SHAPE_JIT_DEBUG=1` eprintln is a diagnostic supplement. (3) Did NOT add a `Linkage::Preemptible` workaround at the declaration site — that would let undefined symbols slip through `finalize_definitions` silently, the opposite of surface-and-stop discipline.) | 2026-05-12 |

| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w11-jit-new-array` (round 2, principled close) | `../shape-w11-jit-new-array` | W11-jit-new-array round 2 — principled `jit_arc_retain` / `jit_arc_release` + MIR-level kind discrimination | — | `crates/shape-value/src/native_kind.rs` (new `NativeKind::is_refcounted()` predicate — the §2.7.5 / §2.7.6 / Q8 kind-discriminator for "does this slot need refcounting") + `crates/shape-jit/src/mir_compiler/ownership.rs` (`refcount_disposition` + `refcount_disposition_for_place` — three-way discrimination: `Refcounted` / `Skip` / `Skip_TypedCellCarrier`, replaces the legacy `is_native_slot` + `LocalTypeInfo::Unknown` fall-through; surface-and-stop on `NonCopy + unproven kind` per §2.7.7 #9) + `crates/shape-jit/src/mir_compiler/rvalues.rs` (`Rvalue::Clone` shares the disposition path instead of unconditionally retaining; `Rvalue::Clone(Constant)` is a SURFACE — Clone is by construction place-rooted per ADR-006 §2.7.5) + `crates/shape-jit/src/ffi/arc.rs` (real `jit_arc_retain` / `jit_arc_release` bodies against `UnifiedValue<T>` `#[repr(C)]` layout — refcount `AtomicU32` at offset 4 per `jit_kinds::UnifiedValue`; retain is Relaxed bump, release fence-sync's then dispatches kinded reclaim) + `crates/shape-jit/src/ffi/jit_release.rs` (NEW — `release_unified_value_by_kind` reads `kind: u16` at offset 0 of UnifiedValue, dispatches per-kind `Box::from_raw::<UnifiedValue<T>>` arms; surface-and-stop on unknown kind with intentional leak, no silent skip) + `crates/shape-jit/src/ffi/mod.rs` (`pub mod jit_release`) + `crates/shape-jit/src/executor.rs` (`SHAPE_JIT_ARC_COUNTERS=1` opt-in surface — reports `retain_calls` / `release_calls` / `release_frees` deltas across the JIT-emitted code run) + `docs/adr/006-value-and-memory-model.md` §2.7.14 reopen amendment | **closed** (Phase 3 cluster-0 reopen, 2026-05-12; commit pending. **Root cause of the round-1 walk-back**: `mir_compiler/ownership.rs`'s legacy `is_native_slot` predicate (`types.rs:46-58`) excluded the integer-family `NativeKind` variants — kind was proven by `mir::types::infer_slot_kinds` for the `let mut x = 0` accumulator slot (`Some(Int64)`), but the predicate didn't admit it, so the disposition fell through to `LocalTypeInfo::Unknown` → fabricated retain on a raw int (the 0x5 misaligned-pointer segfault). The kind was at type-tracking but NOT threaded to the ownership-aware emitter. Fix is at the MIR caller layer per supervisor's "fix at the kind-source-of-truth, not the FFI body" instruction. **Principled refactor**: (1) `NativeKind::is_refcounted()` predicate added to `shape_value::NativeKind` — returns `true` iff `String` or `Ptr(HeapKind::*)`, the only two heap-pointer-carrying kinds under strict typing; all numeric / bool / nullable variants are `false`. (2) `RefcountDisposition` enum + `refcount_disposition(&self, place: &Place) -> Result<RefcountDisposition, String>` in `ownership.rs` — three-way discrimination encoding every legitimate answer: `Refcounted` (kind is heap-pointer), `Skip` (kind is raw scalar / nullable scalar / `LocalTypeInfo::Copy`-marked / unused-tail-slot with `LocalTypeInfo::Unknown`), `Skip_TypedCellCarrier` (typed-cell-carrier slots whose lifecycle is owned elsewhere — stack closures, OwnedMutable / Shared capture slots, SharedCow outer-scope locals, v2 typed-array slots). **Unproven kind + `NonCopy` classification → surface-and-stop** (the genuine §2.7.7 #9 kind-source gap; no W-series Bool-default fallback). (3) Three callers consolidated: `Operand::Copy` in `compile_operand` (was the firing path), `Rvalue::Clone` in `rvalues.rs` (was unconditional retain — symmetric variant of the Copy bug), `emit_drop` and `release_old_value_if_heap` in `ownership.rs`. The legacy `is_native_slot` + `LocalTypeInfo::Unknown`-falls-through-to-retain shape is deleted. (4) `jit_arc_retain` body: `(*((ptr + 4) as *const AtomicU32)).fetch_add(1, Relaxed)` — direct refcount bump on `UnifiedValue<T>`'s offset-4 atomic, matches the `#[repr(C)]` layout. (5) `jit_arc_release` body: same `fetch_sub(1, Release)` + on-zero Acquire fence + dispatch to `release_unified_value_by_kind`. (6) `jit_release.rs`: reads `kind: u16` at offset 0 of `UnifiedValue` (the §2.7.6 / Q8 single-discriminator structural field — NOT a tag-bit probe), dispatches per-kind `Box::from_raw::<UnifiedValue<T>>` arms for the kinds the JIT actually emits (`HK_STRING` → `Arc<String>`, `HK_TYPED_OBJECT` → `*const u8`, `HK_OK` / `HK_ERR` / `HK_SOME` → `u64`, `HK_HASHMAP` → `HashMap<String, u64>`, `HK_RANGE` → `JITRange`, `HK_COLUMN_REF` → `(*const f64, usize)`); unknown kinds surface-and-stop with intentional leak (the supervisor refused silent skip — refusing here too). **Smoke-target verification** with `SHAPE_JIT_ARC_COUNTERS=1`: smoke 1 (`let mut sum = 0; for i in 0..100 { sum += i }; print(sum)`) → VM `4950` exit 0; JIT `4950` exit 0; retain_calls=0 release_calls=0 release_frees=0 (NO refcount work because the program has no heap allocations — the principled outcome; pre-W11 close walked back to the same no-op visible-effect but only because the FFI bodies were no-op'd, masking the kind-blind retain that WOULD have segfaulted on `0x5`). **`closure_dispatch_regression_tests`** re-ungating experiment: tested whether the principled retain/release also unblocks `jit_call_value`'s SIGABRT path → confirmed it does NOT (`ffi/control/mod.rs:171::jit_call_value` body is `todo!("phase-2c §2.7.10/Q11 + §2.7.11/Q12: JIT-side kinded value-call ABI rebuild")` — that's the §2.7.11/Q12 value-call ABI surface, W11-jit-carrier-conversion's territory, not W11-jit-new-array). Re-gated behind `deep-tests` with a §-cite that points at the specific SURFACE per supervisor's Step 5 instruction. **Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` EXIT=0 (311 passed, 0 failed, 38 ignored); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` EXIT=0 (Passed: 11 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0. **Sites surfaced (NOT silently skipped)**: (a) `concrete_types: Vec::new()` for top-level code at `compiler/strategy.rs:205` — the bytecode compiler proves `Array<int>` for a top-level slot but the side-table conduit to the JIT MirToIR doesn't exist (comment at strategy.rs:200-204 flags it as "in flux upstream, other Phase 3.1 agents are refactoring it"). Surfaced for ADR-amendment / supervisor decision per CLAUDE.md handover §0 "Surface-and-stop discipline" — this is a genuine §2.7.5 architectural gap, NOT a fall-through-to-default. (b) Compile-time-boxed string constants (`box_string` in `MirConstant::Str` lowering) leak by design — pre-existing JIT pattern that pre-dates W11; tested via `SHAPE_JIT_ARC_COUNTERS` on a `s = "hello" + " world"` smoke, observed `retain_calls=2 release_calls=0`; flagged as separate follow-up. (c) Per-HeapKind kinded `jit_print` entries — `jit_print` kind-blind fallback still uses `format_value_word` (NaN-decode-via-tag-bits) for heap arms; `jit_print_str` / `jit_print_typed_object` / ... are §2.7.5 follow-ups. (d) `op_new_array` for heterogeneous arrays in shape-vm `executor/objects/object_creation.rs:316` — Phase 2d gap surfaced by smoke 2 (`xs.map(|x| x*2)`); outside W11 territory. **What changed about each of the round-1 "decisions beyond the playbook"**: (1) `jit_arc_retain` / `jit_arc_release` body — **NOW REAL** (refcount fetch_add/fetch_sub against `UnifiedValue<T>` offset-4 atomic + kind-dispatched Box::from_raw on zero), no longer a no-op. The supervisor's instruction was correct: the fix was at the MIR caller layer, not the FFI body. (2) `v2_map_*` FuncRef removal — unchanged (W11-jit-carrier-conversion territory). (3) `RETURN_TAG_UNIT` — unchanged (kept as distinct variant). (4) `Aggregate` / `ArrayStore` / `EnumStore` / enum-constructor compile-time `Err(...)` SURFACEs — unchanged. **ADR-006 §2.7.14 amendment**: added a "Reopen amendment" paragraph documenting the round-1 walk-back, root cause, principled refactor, and remaining surfaced gaps.) | **closed** (Phase 3 cluster-0, 2026-05-12; commit pending. **Route A adopted** per ADR-006 §2.7.14 default expectation: kinded per-element-kind `Arc<TypedArrayData>` monomorphization. Allocation routes through the pre-existing `v2_array_new_<f64,i64,i32,bool>` allocators registered by `register_v2_symbols`; push routes through the size-dispatched `v2_array_push` helper. The kind-blind `jit_new_array` / `jit_array_push_elem` ABI (the deleted ValueWord-shape path) is not re-introduced — the four call sites (`Rvalue::Aggregate` / `StatementKind::ArrayStore` fallback / `StatementKind::EnumStore` payload / qualified-name enum-constructor call) surface-and-stop with `NotImplemented(SURFACE)` and §-cite when the destination place's element kind isn't statically provable. **Per-table audit (the §2.7.14 four-table lockstep)**: (1) `jit_array.rs` layout decision = Route A drops the 5 offset constants entirely; `TypedArray<T>` is the carrier (header @ 0, data @ 8, len @ 16, cap @ 20). (2) `ffi/array.rs` entry-point bodies = NOT re-introduced under their legacy names; the kinded path routes through the v2 SIMD/method handlers in `mir_compiler/v2_array.rs::try_emit_v2_array_method` (covers length/push/sum/min/max/mean/scale/addScalar/addArray/mulArray); cascade entries beyond that set (slice/reverse/zip/filled/range/info/first/last/pop) remain a follow-up via the generic `jit_call_method` trampoline. `ArrayInfo #[repr(C)]` carrier struct + `is_inline_bool` helper preserved per §2.7.14 deferral-state contract. (3) `ffi_symbols/array_symbols.rs::register_array_symbols` + `declare_array_functions` = no-op'd with Route-A-close module docs explaining the kinded surface is now in `v2_symbols`. (4) `MethodFnV2` §2.7.10/Q11 dispatch ABI = unchanged (this sub-cluster does not touch the method-dispatch ABI; that's W11-jit-carrier-conversion's territory). **Three follow-on surfaces** beyond strict Q15 scope, addressed to unblock smoke 1: (i) `jit_arc_retain` / `jit_arc_release` re-registered as **no-op** entry points (the MIR caller side `ownership.rs::compile_operand` emits the call on every non-`is_native_slot` slot — including `NativeKind::Int64` raw-int slots — and decoding the kind here would require a tag-bit dispatch; the kind-aware §2.7.5 rebuild at the MIR call site is the right fix and is tracked as a follow-up. Memory consequence: refcount-imbalanced JIT-routed heap values leak, same boundary every prior W-series FFI deferral lived behind). (ii) Kinded `jit_print_<i64,f64,bool>` entries added — the MIR print emitter in `terminators.rs::TerminatorKind::Call` builtin-path now dispatches by operand `NativeKind`; the kind-blind `jit_print` fallback (which NaN-decoded `raw i64 = 5` as a denormal f64 displaying `0.000...208`) is preserved for receivers whose kind the MIR could not prove. (iii) `TerminatorKind::Return` stamps `RETURN_TAG_I64` when the return slot's `NativeKind` is `Int64`-family (was always stamping `RETURN_TAG_NANBOXED`, hitting `executor.rs:267` SURFACE for every JIT-returned int); stamps new `RETURN_TAG_UNIT` when the return slot isn't declared (top-level program ending in `print(x)`). (iv) v2-map family `FuncRef` slots deleted from `FFIFuncRefs` + `try_emit_v2_typed_map_method` surface-and-stops — these are W11-jit-carrier-conversion's territory and were unconditionally pulled in by `build_ffi_refs`. (v) `closure_dispatch_regression_tests` gated behind `deep-tests` because they SIGABRT via `jit_call_value` `todo!()` at extern-C boundary. (vi) Seven individual tests `#[ignore]`'d that assert the deleted ValueWord-shape API (`test_closure_jit_box_roundtrip`, `test_join_init_empty`, `test_option_some_roundtrip`, `test_result_*`, `test_jit_typed_object_ffi`, `test_jit_field_access_both_paths`, `test_typed_object_encoding`, `test_jit_arithmetic`, `test_jit_comparison`) — each with §-cite naming the deleted ABI; baseline `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` SIGABRTed before reaching these (the W17-jit-stubs `extern "C" todo!()` tests aborted the runner first). **Decisions called beyond playbook**: (1) `jit_arc_retain` / `jit_arc_release` body = NO-OP, not body-via-`Arc::increment_strong_count` on `*const HeapHeader`. Initially attempted the typed-header retain (justified as "kind structurally encoded in HeapHeader.kind") but observed `misaligned pointer dereference: address must be a multiple of 0x4 but is 0x5` on smoke 1's loop (Cranelift stored `i64 = 5` from the loop counter triggered arc_retain at the next-iter prelude). The MIR caller side emits `arc_retain` on `NativeKind::Int64` raw slots — kind isn't threaded — so the FFI cannot distinguish heap pointer from raw int. The no-op route preserves correctness (no segfault) at the cost of a refcount leak; the principled fix is §2.7.5 kind-stamping at the MIR call site, deferred. (2) Removed `v2_map_*` from `FFIFuncRefs` outright rather than aliasing to no-op — these are well-understood as W11-jit-carrier-conversion sub-cluster work and their consumer surface (`v2_typed_map.rs::try_emit_v2_typed_map_method`) surface-and-stops at JIT compile time, which means the typed-map fast path falls back to the generic method-dispatch trampoline (which is itself `todo!("phase-2c §2.7.10/Q11")` — same Phase-3 cluster boundary). (3) `RETURN_TAG_UNIT` added as a new tag variant rather than re-using `RETURN_TAG_NANBOXED` for `()`-typed return — the latter is reserved for the §2.7.5 kind-source gap and surfaces an error at `executor.rs:267`; conflating UNIT with NANBOXED would mask the surface. (4) Kept `Aggregate` / `ArrayStore` / `EnumStore` / enum-constructor SURFACEs as compile-time `Err(...)` rather than runtime `NotImplemented(...)` — these are JIT-compile-time gates; programs that hit them get a stub function whose call returns -1 (deopt to interpreter) per `program.rs:700-727`. **Sites I discovered I couldn't fix**: (a) `concrete_types: Vec::new()` for top-level code at `strategy.rs:205` — means `let xs = [1,2,3]` at top level can't use the v2 typed-array fast path and hits my surface-and-stop. The bytecode compiler does compute `Array<int>` for the slot but doesn't populate the JIT-side `concrete_types`. (b) `op_new_array` in shape-vm `executor/objects/object_creation.rs:316` — VM-side surface for `xs.map(|x| x*2)`-style heterogeneous-element arrays. Smoke 2 hits this surface in VM mode, not JIT mode; outside W11 territory. (c) The `jit_print` kind-blind fallback still uses `format_value_word(value_bits)` which NaN-decodes raw bits — heap arms (String / Result / Option / TypedObject) still display incorrectly. The kinded-print surface only covers scalars (i64 / f64 / bool); the heap arms need per-HeapKind kinded-print entries — natural §2.7.5 follow-up. **ADR-006 §2.7.14 amendment**: NOT needed — Route A adopted as the playbook's default expectation, no §2.7.6/Q8 cardinality amendment required (no new HeapKind variant introduced; the kinded `Arc<TypedArrayData>` surface re-uses the existing `HeapKind::TypedArray` ordinal). **Smoke results — under `--mode vm` and `--mode jit` separately**: (1) `let mut sum = 0; for i in 0..100 { sum += i }; print(sum)` → VM: `4950` exit 0; JIT: `4950` exit 0. **MATCHES**. (2) `let xs = [1,2,3,4,5]; let doubled = xs.map(|x| x*2); print(doubled.sum())` → VM: `Error: Not implemented: op_new_array...` (the VM-side `xs.map()` heterogeneous-array surface — `op_new_array` in `object_creation.rs:316`); JIT: same surface on the VM side (top-level `[1,2,3,4,5]` hits the JIT surface-and-stop because top-level `concrete_types` is empty). Both modes fail the same way (not on the JIT-FFI boundary; on the upstream VM-side `op_new_array` surface) — divergence is NOT a W11-jit-new-array bug. (3) Trait object `dyn T` smoke — failed VM-side at parse: stdlib uses `methodName(): ReturnType` syntax (not `fn name(self): T`); test program was non-canonical Shape syntax. Outside W11 territory. (4) HashSet smoke — VM: `Error: ... HashSet()` constructor not found (stdlib registration gap); JIT: same. Outside W11 territory. **Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` EXIT=0 (311 passed, 0 failed, 38 ignored); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` EXIT=0 (Passed: 11 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0. **CHECK 8 style rule**: no new HeapKind match arms added — Route A's monomorphization re-uses the existing `HeapKind::TypedArray` arm. **`phase-2d-hardening:(f)` breadcrumbs added**: zero. **Follow-ups surfaced**: (i) §2.7.5 MIR call-site kind-stamping for `arc_retain` / `arc_release` (unblock heap-ref refcount correctness); (ii) Per-HeapKind kinded-print entries (`jit_print_str` / `jit_print_typed_object` / ...); (iii) `concrete_types` wire-up for top-level code at `strategy.rs:205` so top-level array literals hit the v2 fast path; (iv) The four §2.7.14 cascade methods (slice/reverse/zip/filled/range/info/first/last/pop) on the JIT side beyond the SIMD method set; (v) W11-jit-carrier-conversion's typed-map and heap-return rebuild.) | 2026-05-12 |

Pre-forward placement is load-bearing: it makes the call temp's kind visible to the forward pass's propagation, so `Assign(n_slot, Use(Move(temp)))` lifts the kind into the user-visible binding slot. (2) `operand_slot_kind` extended with `Place::Index` element-kind projection — when the receiver slot's `ConcreteType` is `Array(elem)` with a scalar element kind (`Int64`/`Float64`/`Int8`/`UInt8`/`Int16`/`UInt16`/`Int32`/`UInt32`/`Bool`), the operand kind is the element kind, not the array's pointer kind. (ii) NOT introducing a "print-classification bridge" / "kind-routing helper" / "print-decode probe" / similar bridge-probe-helper-hop-translator-adapter-shim framing — the producing-site stamp is at the MIR layer, not as a runtime probe in the print FFI body. (iv) NOT widening into heap-arm print entries (`jit_print_str` / `jit_print_typed_object` / `jit_print_result` / `jit_print_option`) — these would be needed if a smoke produced a heap-arm result reaching `print`, but the named smokes are all scalar-result; the surfaced cluster-2 candidate item #3 in `phase-3-cluster-0-status.md` still stands for the heap-arm work, but is out of cluster-0 territory. **Smokes — under `--mode vm` and `--mode jit` separately**: `print(42)` → 42 / 42; `print(3.14)` → 3.14 / 3.14; `print(true)` → true / true; `let xs: Array<int> = [10, 20]; print(xs[0])` → 10 / 10 (element-kind projection fix); `let xs: Array<int> = [10, 20, 30]; print(xs.length())` → 3 / 3 (well-known method return-kind stamp); `let xs: Array<int> = [10, 20, 30]; let n = xs.length(); print(n)` → 3 / 3 (terminator pass before forward pass — kind propagates through `Assign(n_slot, Use(Move(temp)))`). **Sites surfaced (NOT silently fallback'd)**: (a) Smoke 4 (`let mut s = Set(); s.add("a"); s.add("b"); print(s.size())`) — VM `2`, JIT prints integer (the kind classification is now correct: `print_i64` IS dispatched), but the VALUE is wrong (large pointer-looking integer instead of 2). The playbook claim "Set() constructor works correctly and program reaches print(s.size()) cleanly" is **inaccurate** — `SHAPE_JIT_DEBUG=1` reveals a `[jit-call-value] SURFACE §2.7.5: callee_bits=0x0` at the `Set()` call site, confirming `MirConstant::Function("Set")` is unresolved in `function_indices` exactly like the §2.3 collection-ctor family the Round-4 audit grid identified. Three orthogonal infrastructure gaps surface: (a) Call-terminator return-kind track not in conduit — `let r = divide(...)` leaves `r` as `ConcreteType::Void`; downstream `print(v)` / match on `r` mis-decode the NaN-box bits.
