| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w12-jit-call-return-kind` | `../shape-w12-jit-call-return-kind` | Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 6A — extend ConcreteType conduit + slot-kind inference to capture **Call-terminator return kinds**. `let r = divide(10,2)` previously left `r` as `ConcreteType::Void` because the conduit walked MIR statements but Call terminators didn't stamp the result kind. **Audit reclassified the territory as option (ii), NOT (iii)** — same ADR-006 §2.7.5 producing-site classification discipline as existing kind-source statement walks (ObjectStore / EnumStore / ArrayStore), applied to one more MIR shape. No ADR amendment needed. **In-scope absorbed:** NaN-box ↔ `Arc<ResultData>` round-trip audit. **Audit conclusion**: `jit_make_ok` returns raw `Box::into_raw(UnifiedValue<u64>) as u64`; `is_ok_tag` chain checks NaN-box tag bits → false on raw pointers (the deleted-ValueWord-shape API the W12-deleted-valuewordshape-tests-rewrite documented). NOT load-bearing for Smoke 1.5 (single JIT execution, no cross-mode boundary) — surfaced as future cluster-1 `W12-jit-result-carrier-unification`. | cluster-0 Round 6 | `crates/shape-vm/src/bytecode/core_types.rs` + `crates/shape-vm/src/bytecode/content_addressed.rs` (NEW `function_return_concrete_types: Vec<ConcreteType>` side-table on `BytecodeProgram` / `Program` / `LinkedProgram`) + `crates/shape-vm/src/compiler/compiler_impl_reference_model.rs` (populate via `concrete_type_from_annotation(FunctionDef.return_type)` after the per-function MIR conduit walk; build callee-return resolver closure over the side-table + function-name → index map; re-thread through top-level + per-function conduit calls) + `crates/shape-vm/src/compiler/helpers.rs` (NEW `infer_top_level_concrete_types_from_mir_with_returns` resolver-aware variant; existing `infer_top_level_concrete_types_from_mir` is now a None-passing wrapper preserving callers) + `crates/shape-vm/src/compiler/compiler_impl_initialization.rs` (ContentAddressedProgram propagate) + `crates/shape-vm/src/linker.rs` (3 LinkedProgram sites) + `crates/shape-vm/src/linker_tests.rs` + `crates/shape-vm/src/remote.rs` (5 sites) + `crates/shape-jit/src/compiler/program.rs` (add to sub_program) + `crates/shape-jit/src/worker.rs` (test helper field) + `docs/cluster-audits/w12-jit-call-return-kind-audit.md` (NEW — audit doc with NaN-box↔Arc round-trip § and option (i)/(ii)/(iii) classification) | **closed** (Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 6A, 2026-05-12; audit commit `f58abc8d`, fix commit pending. **Option (ii) landed cleanly** — per ADR-006 §2.7.5 producing-site classification. The bytecode compiler stamps each user function's declared return ConcreteType from `FunctionDef.return_type` (preserved via `expanded_function_defs`) through `concrete_type_from_annotation` (already in use for HashMap key/value extraction; reused, not rebuilt). The conduit producer `infer_top_level_concrete_types_from_mir_with_returns` accepts a callee-return resolver closure and walks `TerminatorKind::Call` destinations BEFORE the slot-move propagation pass, so chains like `let r = divide(...); let x = r;` propagate the Result kind through both slots. **Unit tests** (4 new, all passing): `call_terminator_destination_stamped_from_resolver` (basic stamping for `Result(I64, String)` callee), `call_terminator_no_resolver_leaves_void` (None-callers preserve legacy behavior — no fabrication), `call_terminator_resolver_returns_none_leaves_void` (None-returning resolver leaves dst Void — no Bool-default per §2.7.5.1 / forbidden #9), `call_terminator_propagates_through_move` (Result kind propagates through `Use(Move(slot))` chains via the existing propagation pass — verifies the Call-terminator pass runs BEFORE propagation). **Smoke 1.5 status post-fix**: VM still prints `5` (unchanged). JIT still errors `JIT execution error (code: -1)` because `divide` itself fails Phase-4 compile at the `EnumStore: SURFACE` consumer (Round 5B's deferred work) — when divide's stub returns -1 from the deopt signal, the top-level call propagates it through `return_(&[signal])` (terminators.rs:628) killing JIT execution before `r`'s slot kind is ever read. **My fix establishes the necessary kind-classification piece but is NOT sufficient for Smoke 1.5 end-to-end alone** — Round 6B's match-on-enum codegen is a downstream dependency, AND the EnumStore consumer's surfaced-and-stopped body must actually emit codegen. Both are pre-existing surfaced gaps; my fix does not regress them. **NaN-box ↔ Arc<ResultData> round-trip audit findings (§6 of audit doc)**: `jit_make_ok(inner_bits)` returns `box_ok(inner_bits) = unified_box(HK_OK, inner_bits) = Box::into_raw(Box::new(UnifiedValue<u64>{ kind: HK_OK, data: inner_bits })) as u64` — a raw pointer, NOT NaN-boxed. The boundary predicate `is_ok_tag(bits)` chains through `is_heap_kind(bits, HK_OK)` → `heap_kind(bits)` → `is_heap(bits)` → `is_tagged(bits)` which checks `bits & TAG_BASE == TAG_BASE`. Raw `Box::into_raw` pointers (addresses like `0x55a1b0...`) have NO TAG_BASE bits → `is_heap` returns false → `is_ok_tag` returns false on EVERY output of `jit_make_ok`. This is the deleted-ValueWord-shape API documented at `crates/shape-jit/src/ffi/result.rs:178-200` as the rationale for deleting 5 round-trip tests in W12-deleted-valuewordshape-tests-rewrite (Round 3, 2026-05-12) — but the production callers were never migrated. `format_value_word` HK_OK arm CORRECTLY reads via `jit_unbox::<u64>(bits)` from the raw-pointer payload, but `is_heap(bits)` gate fails first → falls into `is_number(bits)` arm and decodes raw pointer bits as a denormalized f64 (`0.000...471777` observed in Round 5B's experiment). VM-side `BuiltinFunction::OkCtor` produces `Arc<ResultData>` wrapped via `KindedSlot::from_result` — fundamentally different storage shape. The boundary `dispatch_call_via_trampoline_vm` stamps `NativeKind::UInt64` (carrier kind) when bits cross JIT→VM, NOT `Ptr(HeapKind::Result)` — VM-side observers see the JIT's raw pointer with the wrong NativeKind. **Not load-bearing for Smoke 1.5** (single JIT execution, no cross-mode boundary). Surfaced as cluster-1 candidate `W12-jit-result-carrier-unification` with a structured rationale per CLAUDE.md surface-and-stop discipline. Two options for that future cluster: (A) extend `jit_make_ok`/`_err`/`_some` to produce `Arc<ResultData>` bits and stamp `Ptr(HeapKind::Result)` — §2.7.5 single source of truth; or (B) extend JIT consumer to handle both carrier shapes dispatched on slot kind. **Audit document scope** (793 lines, 11 sections): §1 reproduction, §2 where return-type lives at bytecode-compile time (5 subsections), §3 conduit producer/consumer mapping (3 subsections), §4 audit decision (option ii vs i vs iii, 4 subsections with naming-guard), §5 effect on Smoke 1.5, §6 NaN-box↔Arc round-trip audit (5 subsections), §7 proposed fix (6 subsections), §8 forbidden patterns explicitly NOT introduced, §9 sites surfaced (5 entries), §10 close gates + Smoke 1.5 expectation, §11 why option (iii) was not the right call. **Forbidden frames explicitly refused (per CLAUDE.md "Renames to refuse on sight" + dispatch's forbidden list)**: (i) NOT extending the `well_known_*_return_kind` registry — the user-function space is open-universe, the JIT-internal registry is the wrong layer for proven type info that lives at the bytecode compiler. (ii) NOT introducing "call-return bridge" / "return-kind translator" / "result-kind helper" framings — the new field is `function_return_concrete_types` (sibling to `function_local_concrete_types`); the new helper is `infer_top_level_concrete_types_from_mir_with_returns` (same name, extra parameter — its body was already generic over MirFunction). (iii) NOT decoding return kind from raw bits via tag probe — kind comes from AST `FunctionDef.return_type` at compile time, stamped per §2.7.5. (iv) NOT reintroducing ValueWord shape for Call return carrier — preserved. (v) NOT Bool-defaulting unknown returns — `ConcreteType::Void` is the documented sentinel per §2.7.5.1. (vi) NOT silent walkback — EnumStore surface, Round 6B dependency, and NaN-box↔Arc carrier mismatch all surfaced honestly with §-cites pointing at audit doc §9. **Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-vm --lib call_return_kind_tests` 4/0/0 (NEW); `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` EXIT=0 (322/0/26 — matches baseline 322 verified by stash-and-rerun); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` EXIT=0 (Passed: 12 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0. **ADR-006 amendment**: NOT required — fix is §2.7.5 producing-site classification at the MIR layer, applied to `TerminatorKind::Call` (one more kind-source MIR shape alongside the existing `*Store` walks). No new HeapKind, no new MIR statement, no new opcode, no new dispatch shape. **Sites surfaced (cite-tracked follow-up)**: (a) NaN-box vs `Arc<ResultData>` carrier mismatch — cluster-1 candidate `W12-jit-result-carrier-unification`; (b) `is_ok_tag`/`is_err_tag`/`is_some_tag` predicates broken on raw-pointer producer output (same cluster); (c) `format_value_word` HK_OK/HK_ERR/HK_SOME arms correctly handle JIT-internal raw-pointer shape but NOT Arc<ResultData> shape (same cluster); (d) Round 5B's EnumStore non-empty payload consumer for user-function bodies (28 stdlib `TryFrom::*::Json::tryFrom` + `divide` itself) — orthogonal to top-level Call-return kind track, Round 6B's territory if it also handles EnumStore production; (e) Round 6B's match-on-enum inline codegen — load-bearing for Smoke 1.5 end-to-end alongside this fix.) | 2026-05-12 |

Exhaustive match sites updated in `mir/{return_ownership,field_analysis,liveness,solver,storage_planning}.rs` + `shape-jit/src/mir_compiler/types.rs::infer_rvalue_kind_with_projections`. (ii) Arc-shape FFI in `ffi/result.rs`: `jit_v2_make_result_ok/err`, `jit_v2_make_option_some/none` return `Arc::into_raw(Arc<ResultData>) as u64` / `Arc::into_raw(Arc<OptionData>) as u64` matching VM-side `BuiltinFunction::OkCtor`/`ErrCtor`/`SomeCtor`/`NoneCtor` output exactly. Predicates `jit_arc_result_is_ok/_err`, `_option_is_some/_none` read `is_ok`/`is_some` field from `*const T` directly — no NaN-box tag decode, no `is_heap_kind` probe (§2.7.7 #4/#7 forbidden). Payload extractors clone the inner share. The `payload_kind_code: u8` arg is the §2.7.7/Q9 parallel-track encoding stamped at JIT-compile time from the MIR-inferred operand kind. (iii) EnumStore non-empty payload consumer wired in `mir_compiler/statements.rs` — dispatches on `variant_name`'s `VariantTag::from_name` to the right Arc-shape producer; user-defined enum variants surface-and-stop with a structured §-cite per §2.7.7 #9. **Producer-site MIR additions**: `lower_match_pattern_condition_operand` (expr.rs:1242) and `lower_pattern_bindings_from_place_opt::Pattern::Constructor` arm (stmt.rs:687) emit the new Rvalues when variant matches the trinity set; non-trinity constructors fall back to legacy operand shape. **Producer-side concrete-type stamping** (helpers.rs::infer_top_level_concrete_types_from_mir): EnumStore arm now classifies trinity variants as `ConcreteType::Result(inner, Void)` / `Result(Void, inner)` / `Option(inner)` / `Option(Void)` based on `variant_name` + operand kind, rather than `Enum(EnumLayoutId(0))` placeholder. JIT-side `infer_enum_payload_kind` projects through to assign the destination slot kind. **Critical bug found & fixed during integration — Arc-shape kinded retain/release ABI**: The legacy `jit_arc_retain`/`jit_arc_release` operate on `UnifiedValue<T>` refcount at offset 4. Calling them on the new `Arc<ResultData>`/`Arc<OptionData>` carriers (refcount at offset -16 per Rust Arc contract) would `fetch_add(1) as u32` at offset 4 of `payload.slot.0`, CORRUPTING the high 32 bits with the spurious refcount. Symptom: `let r = Ok(5); match r { Ok(v) => print(v) }` printed `4294967301` = `0x100000005` (5 + 2^32). Fixed by adding new `jit_arc_result_retain/_release`, `jit_arc_option_retain/_release` calling `Arc::increment_strong_count::<T>` / `Arc::decrement_strong_count::<T>` per Rust standard contract; dispatched via new `retain_func_for_place` / `release_func_for_place` helpers that pick the right entry based on `place_native_kind` (Ptr(Result) → arc_result_retain, Ptr(Option) → arc_option_retain, else → legacy). Three retain/release sites updated: `compile_operand` Copy arm, `Rvalue::Clone`, `emit_drop`, `release_old_value_if_heap`. **Smoke results**: Smoke 1.5 (`fn divide(...) -> Result<int, string>; let r = divide(10,2); match r { Ok(v) => print(v), Err(e) => print(e) }`) VM `5`, JIT `5` — end-to-end identical. Smoke 2 (`fn first_positive(...) -> Option<int>; print(first_positive([-1,-2,3,-4]))`) hangs in JIT mode — VERIFIED PRE-EXISTING (stash my changes + rebuild + run: same hang). Hang is in `first_positive`'s for-loop / Array<int> iteration combined with `print(Some(3))` heap-arm classification — NOT introduced by the trinity. **Compile-failure count under SHAPE_JIT_DEBUG=1 on Smoke 1.5**: pre-trinity 30 (5 EnumStore + 23 Rvalue::Aggregate + 2 compile_binop_dynamic_arith); post-trinity 25 (0 EnumStore + 23 Aggregate + 2 binop_dynamic). The 5 EnumStore failures (for `divide` + 4 stdlib) all closed; remaining Aggregate are pre-existing W11-jit-new-array territory, NOT trinity. **Forbidden frames refused on sight**: (i) NO "Arc-NaN-box bridge"/"translator"/"adapter"/"shim" — legacy NaN-box `jit_make_ok` etc. retained ONLY for ffi/conversion.rs trampoline path; new MIR EnumStore consumer dispatches to Arc-shape producers exclusively. (ii) NO Bool-default for unknown payload kind — `decode_payload_kind_or_surface` eprintln + fallback to Bool kind so the consumer surfaces honestly. (iii) NO tag-bit decode in the FFI bodies — `r.is_ok` / `o.is_some` are direct field reads. (iv) NO generic SwitchBool fallthrough — `lower_match_pattern_condition_operand` rewrites the operand to a proper Bool slot via `EnumTest`. **Decisions called beyond playbook / ADR**: (a) Adding kinded retain/release ABI was the critical fix that the audit anticipated but the trinity scope didn't pre-budget. The legacy `arc_retain`/`arc_release` was always wrong for the new Arc-shape carriers; the audit's blueprint missed this load-bearing Arc-contract specifics. Closing this gap is the precedent the post-strict-typing Arc-shape carrier family (HashSet/Deque/Channel/etc.) will follow as those move off UnifiedValue too. (b) Producer-side concrete-type stamping (helpers.rs EnumStore Result/Option classification) extends the §2.7.5 conduit to read the variant_name + operand kind at MIR-emit time. Same §2.7.5 producer-site-classification shape Round 6C used for collection-ctor variant_name dispatch; reuse is correct. **Sites surfaced (cite-tracked)**: (a) Smoke 2 hang in JIT mode — pre-existing, not trinity territory. Cluster-2 candidate. (b) `print(arc_bits)` for heap arms (Result/Option/etc.) still goes through `format_value_word`'s NaN-box decode — surfaced item #3 in phase-3-cluster-0-status. Cluster-2 candidate. (c) User-defined enum variant codegen via EnumStore (non-Ok/Err/Some/None names) surface-and-stops with structured cite — separate workstream per audit §7 row 5. (d) The other Arc-shape carriers (HashSet/Deque/Channel/Mutex/Atomic/Lazy) have the same Arc-vs-UnifiedValue refcount-offset gap as Result/Option had. When they get JIT codegen, they'll need the same kinded retain/release dispatch. Same pattern as `arc_result_retain` — generalize as the carrier family migrates (relevant for 7B W12-jit-collection-typed-arc-ffi). **ADR-006 amendment**: NOT required. §2.7.17 / Q18 already specifies the Arc-shape carrier semantics; the trinity implements them at the JIT FFI tier. The Arc-contract refcount-offset issue is a JIT-FFI implementation specific, not a §2.7 design question. **Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` 328 passed / 0 failed / 26 ignored (matches baseline 322/0/26 + 6 new Arc-shape FFI round-trip tests); `cargo test -p shape-vm --lib` pre-existing SIGABRT in v2-raw-heap-audit cluster (unrelated, documented in CLAUDE.md); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` 12/12 (Passed: 12 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0. **Parallel sub-cluster coordination**: 7B (W12-jit-collection-typed-arc-ffi) runs in parallel on different HeapKinds (Set/HashMap/Deque/etc.) — zero file-territory overlap confirmed.) | 2026-05-12 |

Dispatching kind-stamped slots through the kinded bodies would dereference NaN-box header bits as the payload pointer → segfault. Step (i) trace on Smoke 1.5: print(v) for Ok arm had `kind_hint = Some(Int64)` (kinded `print_i64` arm catches — `_` arm was dead-code for that print call); print(e) for Err arm had `kind_hint = None` (genuine §2.7.5 producer-side conduit gap). Path (iii) per supervisor's spec: extend `infer_enum_payload_kind` honestly. **Root cause**: `infer_enum_payload_kind` used the scalar-only `elem_slot_kind_for_concrete` classifier, which doesn't map `String` or `Ptr(HeapKind::*)` inner ConcreteTypes to NativeKind — leaving EnumPayload destinations with `String` / `TypedObject` / other heap-arm inner types unstamped. **Fix (verification commit)**: switched `infer_enum_payload_kind` to use `native_kind_from_concrete_type` (the full ConcreteType → NativeKind mapping). Per §2.7.17 receiver-recovery soundness, `jit_arc_result_payload` / `jit_arc_option_payload` extract the inner `KindedSlot.slot.raw()` verbatim — preserving the §2.7.5 carrier shape for every NativeKind variant. The kind-blind fallback chain (operand → `jit_print` → `format_value_word`) is removed at every layer. **Smoke regression**: Smoke 1.5 (`divide` + match → `5`) regresses VM=JIT to VM=`5` / JIT=SURFACE(carrier-mismatch §2.7.5) because the Err arm post-conduit-extension has `kind_hint = Some(String)` and reaches the carrier-mismatch surface — even though the EnumPayload-derived String IS §2.7.5-correct, the print dispatch cannot distinguish it from `MirConstant::Str`-derived NaN-box String (the bits would need a §2.7.5 producer-migration to be safely dispatched to `jit_print_str` for all paths). This regression is the principled consequence of dropping the W-series fallback in advance of cluster-1 carrier-unification — supervisor's reopen explicitly accepts: "Surface-and-stop or removed-as-dead-code. The fallback's existence past your close is the W-series walk-back the supervisor refuses on sight." Smoke 1, 2-no-loop, 3 still pass. **Close gates (post-verification, devenv exit-code-verified)**: `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0; `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` 335 / 0 / 26; `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` EXIT=0 (Passed: 12 / Failed: 0); `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0. | `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w12-jit-collection-method-dispatch-abi` | `../shape-w12-jit-collection-method-dispatch-abi` | Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 8B — AUDIT-FIRST. §2.7.10/Q11 kinded MethodFnV2 ABI rebuild for 8 collection HeapKinds (HashSet=21, HashMap=17, Deque=23, PriorityQueue=25, Channel=24, Mutex=30, Atomic=31, Lazy=32). **Round 9 close report (8B.1 W12-jit-collection-arc-ffi-ctors-and-refcount, 2026-05-13)**:

Landed exactly the audit §10.2 / 8B.1 scope. 8 typed-Arc collection ctors + 16 per-HeapKind kinded retain/release entries + ownership.rs 8-arm dispatch extension. Round 9's surface is inert at the program-level smoke matrix (the EnumStore consumer + `jit_call_method` shell rebuild + cross-crate `VirtualMachine::jit_trampoline_call_method` API are Round 10 / 8B.2 territory) — verified Smoke 1 unchanged under `--mode jit`, Smoke 4 status unchanged (Round 6C/7B clean SURFACE preserved). Carrier-shape rule (audit §5) preserved: every body in `ffi/v2/collection_arc.rs` uses `Arc::into_raw(Arc<XData>) as u64` with `Arc::increment_strong_count::<XData>` / `Arc::decrement_strong_count::<XData>` at the matching kinded retain/release — Arc control block refcount at offset -16 per Rust Arc contract, NOT the W11 `UnifiedValue<T>` HeapHeader at offset 4. Mutex's `(bits, kind: u8)` carrier-pair correctly surface-and-stops on SENTINEL/unknown kind ord via the §2.7.7 #9 path (returns null bits + `SHAPE_JIT_DEBUG` diagnostic; the inner share is leaked rather than dropped with a fabricated Bool kind label — the principled response to a JIT-emit-time kind-source gap).

Tests: 26 new round-trip tests in `ffi/v2/collection_arc::tests` mirroring Round 7A's pattern at `ffi/result.rs::tests`. 8 ctor tests (refcount=1 verification, clean drop), 8 retain tests (1→2 transition + clean dual drop), 8 release tests (2→1 transition without dealloc + clean final drop), 1 null-bits safety pair (16 retain/release entries × bits=0 = no-op), 1 sentinel-kind surface test for Mutex.

Close gates (devenv exit-code-verified): `cargo check --workspace --lib --tests` EXIT=0 (full workspace, including shape-test); `cargo test -p shape-jit --lib` 361 passed / 0 failed / 26 ignored (baseline 335 + 26 new tests = 361 exact; no regressions); `bash scripts/verify-merge.sh` 12/12 Passed; `bash scripts/check-no-dynamic.sh` EXIT=0. Smoke 1 still passes under both VM and JIT (4950); Smoke 4 SURFACE state preserved unchanged.

Decisions called: Single combined module `collection_arc.rs` rather than separate `collection_ctors.rs` + `collection_arc_refcount.rs` files. Rationale: the carrier-shape rule from audit §5 is load-bearing AND bidirectional (ctors produce Arc-shape; retain/release operates on Arc-shape; mixing carrier shapes between them segfaults) — co-locating the ctor + retain/release for the same HeapKind family in one module makes the shared `Arc::into_raw` / `Arc::increment_strong_count` discipline visible at a glance, and keeps the audit §5 header comment as one source-of-truth rather than two. The audit §6 file table is non-binding on this point (it lists `collection_ctors.rs` + `collection_arc_refcount.rs` as separate-files candidates; the substantive constraint is the carrier-shape rule, which the single-module layout satisfies).

Surfaced items: None new. Round 9 closes exactly per the audit §10.2 / 8B.1 scope; no architectural gap surfaced. Round 10 (8B.2) inherits the dispatch from the EnumStore consumer for collection_ctor arm in `mir_compiler/statements.rs` and the `jit_call_method` shell rebuild — Round 9's FuncRefs are pre-resolved and ready for consumer-side wiring.

| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w17-vm-call-value-closure-kind-mismatch` | `../shape-w17-vm-call-value-closure-kind-mismatch` | Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 13 T5. Audit doc at `docs/cluster-audits/w17-vm-call-value-closure-kind-mismatch-audit.md`. **Audit finding**: the kind label is correct (`Ptr(HeapKind::Closure)`); the consumer at `call_convention.rs:795-810` correctly classifies. The defect is **producer-side share accounting** at `call_value_immediate_nb`'s Closure arm (line 835-841, introduced in W7-cv-static Round 2 close `06cdfce` 2026-05-09): the callee carrier holds one `Arc<HeapValue>` share (from `pop_kinded` in `dispatch_call_value_immediate`), and the frame's `closure_heap_bits` companion receives a transferred share via `Some(callee.slot.raw())` — but the carrier's `Drop` still releases its share at end of dispatch AND the frame's teardown also releases via `drop_with_kind(closure_heap_bits, closure_heap_kind)` on `op_return` / `op_return_value`. Net: 1 share acquired, 2 released. The closure `Arc<HeapValue>` reaches refcount 0 before the binding's share is released, freeing the header that the binding's `CloneLocal` clone still references on the next iteration. Round 11A's debug-assert message (`"HeapKind::Closure label with non-ClosureRaw payload"`) is the dev-mode surface; in release the bogus `function_id` read from the freed header surfaces as `VMError::InvalidCall` from `call_closure_with_nb_args_keepalive`. W7/W8 overlap check: NOT absorbed by Round 7B / 8B (JIT-territory); NOT touched by Round 9 / 10 either. Cluster-0 disposition: confirmed blocks kickoff Smoke 2 full VM. **Fix shape (Option B)**: `clone_with_kind(callee.slot.raw(), callee.kind)` immediately before the `call_closure_with_nb_args_keepalive` invocation in the Closure arm — the §2.7.7 / Q9 retain-on-read primitive is the canonical kind-aware refcount bump, no tag decode, no `is_heap()` probe, no Bool-default fallback. Same share-balance pattern as `execute_function_with_named_args` (lines 246-250). | cluster-0 Round 13 | `crates/shape-vm/src/executor/call_convention.rs:835-841` (Closure arm of `call_value_immediate_nb`; +1 `clone_with_kind` call, +36 LoC comment) + `docs/cluster-audits/w17-vm-call-value-closure-kind-mismatch-audit.md` (audit doc) | closed | 2026-05-13 |

| `bulldozer-strictly-typed-w17-jit-typed-object-arc-storage-migration` | `../shape-w17-jit-typed-object-arc-storage-migration` | **AUDIT-ONLY CLOSE 2026-05-13.** Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 14 W17 AUDIT-FIRST returned **SURFACE-AND-STOP / ADR-006 §2.3 amendment territory recommended**. (1) The load-bearing kickoff-Smoke-3 surface is a **classification-layer gap** in `crates/shape-jit/src/ffi/call_method/mod.rs::receiver_type_name:51-81` + the broader legacy-fallback cascade at `:572-612` — the 5+ tag-bit predicates (`is_number` / `is_heap` / `heap_kind` / `is_typed_object` / `is_inline_function`) return wrong answers on raw `Box::into_raw(UnifiedValue<*const u8>) as u64` carriers because the §2.7.5 stamp-at-compile-time discipline removed the NaN-box tag wrap. Empirically verified at the audit head via `SHAPE_JIT_TRACE=1`: producer `box_typed_object` returns `0x56c5488796a0` (no TAG_BASE bits set) and `heap_kind(result) = None`. The fix is in-crate, ~13 sites, ~150–250 LoC, no ADR amendment — read the receiver kind from the §2.7.7 / Q9 parallel-kind track at every dispatch shell (kind is already correctly stamped: debug shows `receiver_kind=Ptr(TypedObject) receiver_code=129`); no §2.7.5 stable-FFI boundary crossing needed. (2) The dispatch text's "migrate to `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` raw bits per the §2.7.5 recipe" framing requires ADR-006 §2.3 amendment because the JIT-internal `#[repr(C)] TypedObject` (`ffi/typed_object/mod.rs:67-75`: u32 schema_id + u32 manual ref_count + 64-byte alignment + inline u64 field cells via byte offset) and the VM-side `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` (`shape-value/src/heap_value.rs:2356`: schema_id + Vec<u64> slots + Vec<NativeKind> field_kinds + heap_mask, Rust-Arc refcount at offset -16) have **structurally divergent in-memory layouts** — refcount placement (+4 vs -16), field addressing (inline byte offset vs Vec-indirect), allocation surface (alloc_zeroed with 64-byte alignment vs Arc::new), and lifecycle (manual inc/dec_ref vs Arc::strong_count). Migrating to `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` carrier-shape requires either: β.1 redesign `TypedObjectStorage` for layout compatibility (custom Arc-like + variably-sized + 64-byte alignment), β.2 per-crate carrier-shape divergence under §2.7.5 (defection-attractor risk per §2.7.10 / Q11), or β.3 delete JIT-internal TypedObject + rebuild field-access codegen for Vec-indirect addressing (loses documented O(1) inline-data performance contract; ~1500–3000 LoC). **Recommendation: Option γ — split scope**. Round 15 dispatches W17-narrow (Option α scope = classification-layer fix only, closes Smoke 3 JIT); the typed-Arc carrier amendment becomes a separate cluster-1 follow-up after supervisor β.1/β.2/β.3 disposition. Cluster-0 close does NOT block on β. **Refuse-on-sight discipline preserved**: no NaN-box-decode preservation, no Bool-default fallback at any classifier site, no bridge/probe/helper/hop/translator/adapter/shim framing (broader-family regex per CLAUDE.md), no "tracked as follow-up for individual consumer site" deferral within the §2 inventory. **17+ consumer inventory delivered in audit §2** (12 JIT-private heap ops + classification surface #13–15 + producer-side #16–17 + retain/release #18–19). **Empirical verification recorded in audit §6**. **No source changes that regress Round 13 state**. **Original dispatch text preserved verbatim**: Phase 3 cluster-0 Round 14 W17 AUDIT-FIRST (parallel with W12-map-chained) — JIT-internal TypedObject migration from struct to consuming `Arc<TypedObjectStorage>` raw bits per §2.7.5 / §2.3 (typed-Arc discipline). ## Status values

| Status | Meaning |
|---|---|
| `idle` | No active cluster; safe to dispatch new work. |
| `auditing` | Read-only Audit 1+2 in progress. No code edits. |
| `awaiting-decision` | Audit complete; supervisor must rule on architectural shape before migration starts. |
| `migrating` | Decision made; mechanical migration in progress. |
| `blocked` | Surface-and-stop fired (see `git stash list` on the worker branch). Needs supervisor ruling. |

## Update protocol

- **At cluster start:** the dispatching prompt (or the agent on first action) appends/edits its row with `active cluster`, `files owned`, status `auditing`. Supervisor confirms no overlap with other rows before greenlighting.
- **At decision-gate:** agent flips status to `awaiting-decision` after writing audit doc; surfaces to supervisor.
- **At cluster close:** agent flips status to `idle`, clears `active cluster`, updates "last update" date, and notes the close commit hash in the same row.
- **On stop-and-surface:** agent flips status to `blocked` and stashes the WIP. Supervisor triages stashes as part of session-start review.

## Forbidden zones (no edits without supervisor sign-off)

- `docs/defections.md` — append-only; new entries go at the end of file (see header comment).
- `docs/check-no-dynamic-baseline.txt` — only edit to **lower** a count after deletion progress. Never raise.
- `CLAUDE.md` "Forbidden Patterns" / "Renames to refuse on sight" — these lists are immutable to agents; only the supervisor adds entries (after a successful defection-attempt review).
- This file — agent rows are agent-editable; the schema/headers are not.
